3485         generic_sig_index = parse_generic_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK_0);
3486 
3487       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
3488         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
3489           classfile_parse_error(
3490             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3491         }
3492         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3493         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
3494 
3495         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible annotation");
3496         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3497         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3498 
3499       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3500         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3501           classfile_parse_error(
3502             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3503         }
3504         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3505         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3506           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3507           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3508           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible annotation");
3509         }
3510         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3511 
3512       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3513         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3514           classfile_parse_error(
3515             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3516         }
3517         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3518         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3519 
3520         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible type annotation");
3521         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3522         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length);
3523 
3524       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3525         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3526           classfile_parse_error(
3527             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3528         }
3529         runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3530         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3531           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3532           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3533           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible type annotation");
3534         }
3535         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3536 
3537       } else {
3538         // Skip unknown attributes
3539         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3540       }
3541       calculate_attr_size += attribute_length;
3542     } // End of attributes For loop
3543 
3544     AnnotationArray* annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3545                                                         runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3546                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations,
3547                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3548                                                         CHECK_0);
3549     AnnotationArray* type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3550                                                              runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3551                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3552                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3553                                                              CHECK_0);
3554 
3555     RecordComponent* record_component =
3556       RecordComponent::allocate(_loader_data, name_index, descriptor_index,
3557                                 attributes_count, generic_sig_index,
3558                                 annotations, type_annotations, CHECK_0);
3559     record_components->at_put(x, record_component);
3560   }  // End of component processing loop
3561 
3562   // Restore buffer's current position.
3563   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3564   return calculate_attr_size;
3565 }
3566 
3567 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(TRAPS) {
3568   set_class_synthetic_flag(true);
3569 }
3570 
3571 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_signature_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs, TRAPS) {
3572   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3573 
3574   const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2(CHECK);
3575   check_property(
3576     valid_symbol_at(signature_index),
3577     "Invalid constant pool index %u in Signature attribute in class file %s",
3578     signature_index, CHECK);
3579   set_class_generic_signature_index(signature_index);
3580 }
3581 
3582 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3583                                                                   ConstantPool* cp,
3584                                                                   u4 attribute_byte_length,
3585                                                                   TRAPS) {
3586   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3587   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3588 
3589   const u1* const current_start = cfs->current();
3590 
3591   guarantee_property(attribute_byte_length >= sizeof(u2),
3592                      "Invalid BootstrapMethods attribute length %u in class file %s",
3593                      attribute_byte_length,
3594                      CHECK);
3595 
3596   cfs->guarantee_more(attribute_byte_length, CHECK);
3597 
3598   const int attribute_array_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3599 
3600   guarantee_property(_max_bootstrap_specifier_index < attribute_array_length,
3601                      "Short length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3602                      CHECK);
3603 
3604 
3605   // The attribute contains a counted array of counted tuples of shorts,
3606   // represending bootstrap specifiers:
3607   //    length*{bootstrap_method_index, argument_count*{argument_index}}
3608   const int operand_count = (attribute_byte_length - sizeof(u2)) / sizeof(u2);
3609   // operand_count = number of shorts in attr, except for leading length
3610 
3611   // The attribute is copied into a short[] array.
3612   // The array begins with a series of short[2] pairs, one for each tuple.
3613   const int index_size = (attribute_array_length * 2);
3614 
3615   Array<u2>* const operands =
3616     MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, index_size + operand_count, CHECK);
3617 
3618   // Eagerly assign operands so they will be deallocated with the constant
3619   // pool if there is an error.
3620   cp->set_operands(operands);
3621 
3622   int operand_fill_index = index_size;
3623   const int cp_size = cp->length();
3624 
3625   for (int n = 0; n < attribute_array_length; n++) {
3626     // Store a 32-bit offset into the header of the operand array.
3627     ConstantPool::operand_offset_at_put(operands, n, operand_fill_index);
3628 
3629     // Read a bootstrap specifier.
3630     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * 2, CHECK);  // bsm, argc
3631     const u2 bootstrap_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3632     const u2 argument_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3633     check_property(
3634       valid_cp_range(bootstrap_method_index, cp_size) &&
3635       cp->tag_at(bootstrap_method_index).is_method_handle(),
3636       "bootstrap_method_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3637       bootstrap_method_index,
3638       CHECK);
3639 
3640     guarantee_property((operand_fill_index + 1 + argument_count) < operands->length(),
3641       "Invalid BootstrapMethods num_bootstrap_methods or num_bootstrap_arguments value in class file %s",
3642       CHECK);
3643 
3644     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, bootstrap_method_index);
3645     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_count);
3646 
3647     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * argument_count, CHECK);  // argv[argc]
3648     for (int j = 0; j < argument_count; j++) {
3649       const u2 argument_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3650       check_property(
3651         valid_cp_range(argument_index, cp_size) &&
3652         cp->tag_at(argument_index).is_loadable_constant(),
3653         "argument_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3654         argument_index,
3655         CHECK);
3656       operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_index);
3657     }
3658   }
3659   guarantee_property(current_start + attribute_byte_length == cfs->current(),
3660                      "Bad length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3661                      CHECK);
3662 }
3663 
3664 bool ClassFileParser::supports_sealed_types() {
3665   return _major_version == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
3666          _minor_version == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
3667          Arguments::enable_preview();
3668 }
3669 
3670 bool ClassFileParser::supports_records() {
3671   return _major_version == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
3672          _minor_version == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
3673          Arguments::enable_preview();
3674 }
3675 
3676 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_attributes(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3677                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
3678                  ClassFileParser::ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
3679                                                  TRAPS) {
3680   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3681   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3682   assert(parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
3683 
3684   // Set inner classes attribute to default sentinel
3685   _inner_classes = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3686   // Set nest members attribute to default sentinel
3687   _nest_members = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3688   // Set _permitted_subclasses attribute to default sentinel
3689   _permitted_subclasses = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3690   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // attributes_count
3691   u2 attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3692   bool parsed_sourcefile_attribute = false;
3693   bool parsed_innerclasses_attribute = false;
3694   bool parsed_nest_members_attribute = false;
3695   bool parsed_permitted_subclasses_attribute = false;
3696   bool parsed_nest_host_attribute = false;
3697   bool parsed_record_attribute = false;
3698   bool parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = false;
3699   bool parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = false;
3700   const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
3701   int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
3702   const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
3703   int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
3704   const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
3705   int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3706   const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
3707   int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3708   bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
3709   bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
3710   bool parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = false;
3711   const u1* inner_classes_attribute_start = NULL;
3712   u4  inner_classes_attribute_length = 0;
3713   u2  enclosing_method_class_index = 0;
3714   u2  enclosing_method_method_index = 0;
3715   const u1* nest_members_attribute_start = NULL;
3716   u4  nest_members_attribute_length = 0;
3717   const u1* record_attribute_start = NULL;
3718   u4  record_attribute_length = 0;
3719   const u1* permitted_subclasses_attribute_start = NULL;
3720   u4  permitted_subclasses_attribute_length = 0;
3721 
3722   // Iterate over attributes
3723   while (attributes_count--) {
3724     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK);  // attribute_name_index, attribute_length
3725     const u2 attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3726     const u4 attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
3727     check_property(
3728       valid_symbol_at(attribute_name_index),
3729       "Attribute name has bad constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3730       attribute_name_index, CHECK);
3731     const Symbol* const tag = cp->symbol_at(attribute_name_index);
3732     if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_file()) {
3733       // Check for SourceFile tag
3734       if (_need_verify) {
3735         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong SourceFile attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3736       }
3737       if (parsed_sourcefile_attribute) {
3738         classfile_parse_error("Multiple SourceFile attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3739       } else {
3740         parsed_sourcefile_attribute = true;
3741       }
3742       parse_classfile_sourcefile_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3743     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_debug_extension()) {
3744       // Check for SourceDebugExtension tag
3745       if (parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist) {
3746           classfile_parse_error(
3747             "Multiple SourceDebugExtension attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3748       }
3749       parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = true;
3750       parse_classfile_source_debug_extension_attribute(cfs, (int)attribute_length, CHECK);
3751     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_inner_classes()) {
3752       // Check for InnerClasses tag
3753       if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute) {
3754         classfile_parse_error("Multiple InnerClasses attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3755       } else {
3756         parsed_innerclasses_attribute = true;
3757       }
3758       inner_classes_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3759       inner_classes_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3760       cfs->skip_u1(inner_classes_attribute_length, CHECK);
3761     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_synthetic()) {
3762       // Check for Synthetic tag
3763       // Shouldn't we check that the synthetic flags wasn't already set? - not required in spec
3764       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3765         classfile_parse_error(
3766           "Invalid Synthetic classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3767           attribute_length, CHECK);
3768       }
3769       parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(CHECK);
3770     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_deprecated()) {
3771       // Check for Deprecatd tag - 4276120
3772       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3773         classfile_parse_error(
3774           "Invalid Deprecated classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3775           attribute_length, CHECK);
3776       }
3777     } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3778       if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
3779         if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
3780           classfile_parse_error(
3781             "Multiple Signature attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3782         }
3783         if (attribute_length != 2) {
3784           classfile_parse_error(
3785             "Wrong Signature attribute length %u in class file %s",
3786             attribute_length, CHECK);
3787         }
3788         parse_classfile_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3789       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
3790         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
3791           classfile_parse_error(
3792             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3793         }
3794         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3795         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
3796         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null visible annotations");
3797         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK);
3798         parse_annotations(cp,
3799                           runtime_visible_annotations,
3800                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3801                           parsed_annotations,
3802                           _loader_data,
3803                           _can_access_vm_annotations,
3804                           CHECK);
3805         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3806       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3807         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3808           classfile_parse_error(
3809             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3810         }
3811         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3812         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3813           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3814           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3815           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null invisible annotations");
3816         }
3817         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3818       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_enclosing_method()) {
3819         if (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3820           classfile_parse_error("Multiple EnclosingMethod attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3821         } else {
3822           parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = true;
3823         }
3824         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 4,
3825           "Wrong EnclosingMethod attribute length %u in class file %s",
3826           attribute_length, CHECK);
3827         cfs->guarantee_more(4, CHECK);  // class_index, method_index
3828         enclosing_method_class_index  = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3829         enclosing_method_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3830         if (enclosing_method_class_index == 0) {
3831           classfile_parse_error("Invalid class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3832         }
3833         // Validate the constant pool indices and types
3834         check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(enclosing_method_class_index),
3835           "Invalid or out-of-bounds class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3836         if (enclosing_method_method_index != 0 &&
3837             (!cp->is_within_bounds(enclosing_method_method_index) ||
3838              !cp->tag_at(enclosing_method_method_index).is_name_and_type())) {
3839           classfile_parse_error("Invalid or out-of-bounds method index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3840         }
3841       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_bootstrap_methods() &&
3842                  _major_version >= Verifier::INVOKEDYNAMIC_MAJOR_VERSION) {
3843         if (parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute) {
3844           classfile_parse_error("Multiple BootstrapMethods attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3845         }
3846         parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = true;
3847         parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(cfs, cp, attribute_length, CHECK);
3848       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3849         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3850           classfile_parse_error(
3851             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3852         }
3853         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3854         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3855         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null visible type annotations");
3856         // No need for the VM to parse Type annotations
3857         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK);
3858       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3859         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3860           classfile_parse_error(
3861             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3862         } else {
3863           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3864         }
3865         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3866           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3867           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3868           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null invisible type annotations");
3869         }
3870         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3871       } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION) {
3872         if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_members()) {
3873           // Check for NestMembers tag
3874           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3875             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3876           } else {
3877             parsed_nest_members_attribute = true;
3878           }
3879           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3880             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestHost and NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3881           }
3882           nest_members_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3883           nest_members_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3884           cfs->skip_u1(nest_members_attribute_length, CHECK);
3885         } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_host()) {
3886           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3887             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3888           } else {
3889             parsed_nest_host_attribute = true;
3890           }
3891           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3892             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestMembers and NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3893           }
3894           if (_need_verify) {
3895             guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong NestHost attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3896           }
3897           cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);
3898           u2 class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3899           check_property(
3900                          valid_klass_reference_at(class_info_index),
3901                          "Nest-host class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3902                          class_info_index, CHECK);
3903           _nest_host = class_info_index;
3904         } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION) {
3905           if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_record()) {
3906             // Skip over Record attribute if not supported or if super class is
3907             // not java.lang.Record.
3908             if (supports_records() &&
3909                 cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index) == vmSymbols::java_lang_Record()) {
3910               if (parsed_record_attribute) {
3911                 classfile_parse_error("Multiple Record attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3912               }
3913               // Check that class is final and not abstract.
3914               if (!_access_flags.is_final() || _access_flags.is_abstract()) {
3915                 classfile_parse_error("Record attribute in non-final or abstract class file %s", CHECK);
3916               }
3917               parsed_record_attribute = true;
3918               record_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3919               record_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3920             } else if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, record)) {
3921               // Log why the Record attribute was ignored.  Note that if the
3922               // class file version is JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION.65535 and
3923               // --enable-preview wasn't specified then a java.lang.UnsupportedClassVersionError
3924               // exception would have been thrown.
3925               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
3926               if (supports_records()) {
3927                 log_info(class, record)(
3928                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because super type is not java.lang.Record",
3929                   _class_name->as_C_string());
3930               } else {
3931                 log_info(class, record)(
3932                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because class file version is not %d.65535",
3933                    _class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
3934               }
3935             }
3936             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3937           } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_15_VERSION) {
3938             // Check for PermittedSubclasses tag
3939             if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_permitted_subclasses()) {
3940               if (supports_sealed_types()) {
3941                 if (parsed_permitted_subclasses_attribute) {
3942                   classfile_parse_error("Multiple PermittedSubclasses attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3943                 }
3944                 // Classes marked ACC_FINAL cannot have a PermittedSubclasses attribute.
3945                 if (_access_flags.is_final()) {
3946                   classfile_parse_error("PermittedSubclasses attribute in final class file %s", CHECK);
3947                 }
3948                 parsed_permitted_subclasses_attribute = true;
3949                 permitted_subclasses_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3950                 permitted_subclasses_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3951               }
3952               cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3953             } else {
3954               // Unknown attribute
3955               cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3956             }
3957           } else {
3958             // Unknown attribute
3959             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3960           }
3961         } else {
3962           // Unknown attribute
3963           cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3964         }
3965       } else {
3966         // Unknown attribute
3967         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3968       }
3969     } else {
3970       // Unknown attribute
3971       cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3972     }
3973   }
3974   _class_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3975                                             runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3976                                             runtime_invisible_annotations,
3977                                             runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3978                                             CHECK);
3979   _class_type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3980                                                  runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3981                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3982                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3983                                                  CHECK);
3984 
3985   if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute || parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3986     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_inner_classes_attribute(
3987                             cfs,
3988                             inner_classes_attribute_start,
3989                             parsed_innerclasses_attribute,
3990                             enclosing_method_class_index,
3991                             enclosing_method_method_index,
3992                             CHECK);
3993     if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute && _need_verify && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3994       guarantee_property(
3995         inner_classes_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + 4 * sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
3996         "Wrong InnerClasses attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3997     }
3998   }
3999 
4000   if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
4001     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_nest_members_attribute(
4002                             cfs,
4003                             nest_members_attribute_start,
4004                             CHECK);
4005     if (_need_verify) {
4006       guarantee_property(
4007         nest_members_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
4008         "Wrong NestMembers attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
4009     }
4010   }
4011 
4012   if (parsed_record_attribute) {
4013     const unsigned int calculated_attr_length = parse_classfile_record_attribute(
4014                             cfs,
4015                             cp,
4016                             record_attribute_start,
4017                             CHECK);
4018     if (_need_verify) {
4019       guarantee_property(record_attribute_length == calculated_attr_length,
4020                          "Record attribute has wrong length in class file %s",
4021                          CHECK);
4022     }
4023   }
4024 
4025   if (parsed_permitted_subclasses_attribute) {
4026     const u2 num_subclasses = parse_classfile_permitted_subclasses_attribute(
4027                             cfs,
4028                             permitted_subclasses_attribute_start,
4029                             CHECK);
4030     if (_need_verify) {
4031       guarantee_property(
4032         permitted_subclasses_attribute_length == sizeof(num_subclasses) + sizeof(u2) * num_subclasses,
4033         "Wrong PermittedSubclasses attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
4034     }
4035   }
4036 
4037   if (_max_bootstrap_specifier_index >= 0) {
4038     guarantee_property(parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute,
4039                        "Missing BootstrapMethods attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
4040   }
4041 }
4042 
4043 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_attributes(InstanceKlass* k) {
4044   assert(k != NULL, "invariant");
4045 
4046   if (_synthetic_flag)
4047     k->set_is_synthetic();
4048   if (_sourcefile_index != 0) {
4049     k->set_source_file_name_index(_sourcefile_index);
4050   }
4051   if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
4052     k->set_generic_signature_index(_generic_signature_index);
4053   }
4054   if (_sde_buffer != NULL) {
4055     k->set_source_debug_extension(_sde_buffer, _sde_length);
4056   }
4057 }
4058 
4059 // Create the Annotations object that will
4060 // hold the annotations array for the Klass.
4061 void ClassFileParser::create_combined_annotations(TRAPS) {
4062     if (_class_annotations == NULL &&
4063         _class_type_annotations == NULL &&
4064         _fields_annotations == NULL &&
4065         _fields_type_annotations == NULL) {
4066       // Don't create the Annotations object unnecessarily.
4067       return;
4068     }
4069 
4070     Annotations* const annotations = Annotations::allocate(_loader_data, CHECK);
4071     annotations->set_class_annotations(_class_annotations);
4072     annotations->set_class_type_annotations(_class_type_annotations);
4073     annotations->set_fields_annotations(_fields_annotations);
4074     annotations->set_fields_type_annotations(_fields_type_annotations);
4075 
4076     // This is the Annotations object that will be
4077     // assigned to InstanceKlass being constructed.
4078     _combined_annotations = annotations;
4079 
4080     // The annotations arrays below has been transfered the
4081     // _combined_annotations so these fields can now be cleared.
4082     _class_annotations       = NULL;
4083     _class_type_annotations  = NULL;
4084     _fields_annotations      = NULL;
4085     _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
4086 }
4087 
4088 // Transfer ownership of metadata allocated to the InstanceKlass.
4089 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_metadata(
4090                                             InstanceKlass* this_klass,
4091                                             int java_fields_count,
4092                                             TRAPS) {
4093   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
4094 
4095   _cp->set_pool_holder(this_klass);
4096   this_klass->set_constants(_cp);
4097   this_klass->set_fields(_fields, java_fields_count);
4098   this_klass->set_methods(_methods);
4099   this_klass->set_inner_classes(_inner_classes);
4100   this_klass->set_nest_members(_nest_members);
4101   this_klass->set_nest_host_index(_nest_host);
4102   this_klass->set_annotations(_combined_annotations);
4103   this_klass->set_permitted_subclasses(_permitted_subclasses);
4104   this_klass->set_record_components(_record_components);
4105   // Delay the setting of _local_interfaces and _transitive_interfaces until after
4106   // initialize_supers() in fill_instance_klass(). It is because the _local_interfaces could
4107   // be shared with _transitive_interfaces and _transitive_interfaces may be shared with
4108   // its _super. If an OOM occurs while loading the current klass, its _super field
4109   // may not have been set. When GC tries to free the klass, the _transitive_interfaces
4110   // may be deallocated mistakenly in InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(). Subsequent
4111   // dereferences to the deallocated _transitive_interfaces will result in a crash.
4112 
4113   // Clear out these fields so they don't get deallocated by the destructor
4114   clear_class_metadata();
4115 }
4116 
4117 AnnotationArray* ClassFileParser::assemble_annotations(const u1* const runtime_visible_annotations,
4118                                                        int runtime_visible_annotations_length,
4119                                                        const u1* const runtime_invisible_annotations,
4120                                                        int runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4121                                                        TRAPS) {
4122   AnnotationArray* annotations = NULL;
4123   if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL ||
4124       runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4125     annotations = MetadataFactory::new_array<u1>(_loader_data,
4126                                           runtime_visible_annotations_length +
4127                                           runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4128                                           CHECK_(annotations));
4129     if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
4130       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_visible_annotations_length; i++) {
4131         annotations->at_put(i, runtime_visible_annotations[i]);
4132       }
4133     }
4134     if (runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4135       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_invisible_annotations_length; i++) {
4136         int append = runtime_visible_annotations_length+i;
4137         annotations->at_put(append, runtime_invisible_annotations[i]);
4138       }
4139     }
4140   }
4141   return annotations;
4142 }
4143 
4144 const InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::parse_super_class(ConstantPool* const cp,
4145                                                         const int super_class_index,
4146                                                         const bool need_verify,
4147                                                         TRAPS) {
4148   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4149   const InstanceKlass* super_klass = NULL;
4150 
4151   if (super_class_index == 0) {
4152     check_property(_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()
4153                    || (_access_flags.get_flags() & JVM_ACC_VALUE),
4154                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4155                    super_class_index,
4156                    CHECK_NULL);
4157   } else {
4158     check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(super_class_index),
4159                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4160                    super_class_index,
4161                    CHECK_NULL);
4162     // The class name should be legal because it is checked when parsing constant pool.
4163     // However, make sure it is not an array type.
4164     bool is_array = false;
4165     if (cp->tag_at(super_class_index).is_klass()) {
4166       super_klass = InstanceKlass::cast(cp->resolved_klass_at(super_class_index));
4167       if (need_verify)
4168         is_array = super_klass->is_array_klass();
4169     } else if (need_verify) {
4170       is_array = (cp->klass_name_at(super_class_index)->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY);
4171     }
4172     if (need_verify) {
4173       guarantee_property(!is_array,
4174                         "Bad superclass name in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
4175     }
4176   }
4177   return super_klass;
4178 }
4179 
4180 #ifndef PRODUCT
4181 static void print_field_layout(const Symbol* name,
4182                                Array<u2>* fields,
4183                                ConstantPool* cp,
4184                                int instance_size,
4185                                int instance_fields_start,
4186                                int instance_fields_end,
4187                                int static_fields_end) {
4188 
4189   assert(name != NULL, "invariant");
4190 
4191   tty->print("%s: field layout\n", name->as_klass_external_name());
4192   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_start, "--- instance fields start ---");
4193   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4194     if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4195       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4196         fs.offset(),
4197         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4198         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4199     }
4200   }
4201   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_end, "--- instance fields end ---");
4202   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_size * wordSize, "--- instance ends ---");
4203   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields(), "--- static fields start ---");
4204   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4205     if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4206       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4207         fs.offset(),
4208         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4209         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4210     }
4211   }
4212   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", static_fields_end, "--- static fields end ---");
4213   tty->print("\n");
4214 }
4215 #endif
4216 
4217 OopMapBlocksBuilder::OopMapBlocksBuilder(unsigned int max_blocks) {
4218   _max_nonstatic_oop_maps = max_blocks;
4219   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = 0;
4220   if (max_blocks == 0) {
4221     _nonstatic_oop_maps = NULL;
4222   } else {
4223     _nonstatic_oop_maps =
4224         NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4225     memset(_nonstatic_oop_maps, 0, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * max_blocks);
4226   }
4227 }
4228 
4229 OopMapBlock* OopMapBlocksBuilder::last_oop_map() const {
4230   assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0, "Has no oop maps");
4231   return _nonstatic_oop_maps + (_nonstatic_oop_map_count - 1);
4232 }
4233 
4234 // addition of super oop maps
4235 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::initialize_inherited_blocks(OopMapBlock* blocks, unsigned int nof_blocks) {
4236   assert(nof_blocks && _nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0 &&
4237          nof_blocks <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "invariant");
4238 
4239   memcpy(_nonstatic_oop_maps, blocks, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * nof_blocks);
4240   _nonstatic_oop_map_count += nof_blocks;
4241 }
4242 
4243 // collection of oops
4244 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::add(int offset, int count) {
4245   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0) {
4246     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4247   }
4248   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4249   if (nonstatic_oop_map->count() == 0) {  // Unused map, set it up
4250     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4251     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4252   } else if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(offset)) { // contiguous, add
4253     nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(count);
4254   } else { // Need a new one...
4255     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4256     assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "range check");
4257     nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4258     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4259     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4260   }
4261 }
4262 
4263 // general purpose copy, e.g. into allocated instanceKlass
4264 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::copy(OopMapBlock* dst) {
4265   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count != 0) {
4266     memcpy(dst, _nonstatic_oop_maps, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4267   }
4268 }
4269 
4270 // Sort and compact adjacent blocks
4271 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::compact() {
4272   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= 1) {
4273     return;
4274   }
4275   /*
4276    * Since field layout sneeks in oops before values, we will be able to condense
4277    * blocks. There is potential to compact between super, own refs and values
4278    * containing refs.
4279    *
4280    * Currently compaction is slightly limited due to values being 8 byte aligned.
4281    * This may well change: FixMe if it doesn't, the code below is fairly general purpose
4282    * and maybe it doesn't need to be.
4283    */
4284   qsort(_nonstatic_oop_maps, _nonstatic_oop_map_count, sizeof(OopMapBlock),
4285         (_sort_Fn)OopMapBlock::compare_offset);
4286   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count < 2) {
4287     return;
4288   }
4289 
4290   // Make a temp copy, and iterate through and copy back into the original
4291   ResourceMark rm;
4292   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy =
4293       NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4294   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy_end = oop_maps_copy + _nonstatic_oop_map_count;
4295   copy(oop_maps_copy);
4296   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4297   unsigned int new_count = 1;
4298   oop_maps_copy++;
4299   while(oop_maps_copy < oop_maps_copy_end) {
4300     assert(nonstatic_oop_map->offset() < oop_maps_copy->offset(), "invariant");
4301     if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(oop_maps_copy->offset())) {
4302       nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4303     } else {
4304       nonstatic_oop_map++;
4305       new_count++;
4306       nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(oop_maps_copy->offset());
4307       nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4308     }
4309     oop_maps_copy++;
4310   }
4311   assert(new_count <= _nonstatic_oop_map_count, "end up with more maps after compact() ?");
4312   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = new_count;
4313 }
4314 
4315 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_on(outputStream* st) const {
4316   st->print_cr("  OopMapBlocks: %3d  /%3d", _nonstatic_oop_map_count, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4317   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
4318     OopMapBlock* map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4319     OopMapBlock* last_map = last_oop_map();
4320     assert(map <= last_map, "Last less than first");
4321     while (map <= last_map) {
4322       st->print_cr("    Offset: %3d  -%3d Count: %3d", map->offset(),
4323                    map->offset() + map->offset_span() - heapOopSize, map->count());
4324       map++;
4325     }
4326   }
4327 }
4328 
4329 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_value_on(outputStream* st) const {
4330   print_on(st);
4331 }
4332 
4333 void ClassFileParser::throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_DECL,
4334                                                 const char* msg,
4335                                                 const Symbol* name,
4336                                                 const Symbol* sig) const {
4337 
4338   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
4339   if (name == NULL || sig == NULL) {
4340     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4341         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4342         "class: %s - %s", _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4343   }
4344   else {
4345     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4346         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4347         "\"%s\" sig: \"%s\" class: %s - %s", name->as_C_string(), sig->as_C_string(),
4348         _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4349   }
4350 }
4351 
4352 // Layout fields and fill in FieldLayoutInfo.  Could use more refactoring!
4353 void ClassFileParser::layout_fields(ConstantPool* cp,
4354                                     const FieldAllocationCount* fac,
4355                                     const ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
4356                                     FieldLayoutInfo* info,
4357                                     TRAPS) {
4358 
4359   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4360 
4361   // Field size and offset computation
4362   int nonstatic_field_size = _super_klass == NULL ? 0 :
4363                                _super_klass->nonstatic_field_size();
4364   int next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = 0;
4365   int first_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = 0;
4366 
4367   // Fields that are inline types are handled differently depending if they are static or not:
4368   // - static fields are oops
4369   // - non-static fields are embedded
4370 
4371   // Count the contended fields by type.
4372   //
4373   // We ignore static fields, because @Contended is not supported for them.
4374   // The layout code below will also ignore the static fields.
4375   int nonstatic_contended_count = 0;
4376   FieldAllocationCount fac_contended;
4377   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4378     FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4379     if (fs.is_contended()) {
4380       fac_contended.count[atype]++;
4381       if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4382         nonstatic_contended_count++;
4383       }
4384     }
4385   }
4386 
4387 
4388   // Calculate the starting byte offsets
4389   int next_static_oop_offset    = InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields();
4390   // Inline types in static fields are not embedded, they are handled with oops
4391   int next_static_double_offset = next_static_oop_offset +
4392                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + fac->count[STATIC_INLINE]) * heapOopSize);
4393   if (fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) {
4394     next_static_double_offset = align_up(next_static_double_offset, BytesPerLong);
4395   }
4396 
4397   int next_static_word_offset   = next_static_double_offset +
4398                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) * BytesPerLong);
4399   int next_static_short_offset  = next_static_word_offset +
4400                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_WORD]) * BytesPerInt);
4401   int next_static_byte_offset   = next_static_short_offset +
4402                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_SHORT]) * BytesPerShort);
4403 
4404   int nonstatic_fields_start  = instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() +
4405                                 nonstatic_field_size * heapOopSize;
4406 
4407   // First field of inline types is aligned on a long boundary in order to ease
4408   // in-lining of inline types (with header removal) in packed arrays and
4409   // inlined fields
4410   int initial_inline_type_padding = 0;
4411   if (is_inline_type()) {
4412     int old = nonstatic_fields_start;
4413     nonstatic_fields_start = align_up(nonstatic_fields_start, BytesPerLong);
4414     initial_inline_type_padding = nonstatic_fields_start - old;
4415   }
4416 
4417   int next_nonstatic_field_offset = nonstatic_fields_start;
4418 
4419   const bool is_contended_class     = parsed_annotations->is_contended();
4420 
4421   // Class is contended, pad before all the fields
4422   if (is_contended_class) {
4423     next_nonstatic_field_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4424   }
4425 
4426   // Temporary inline types restrictions
4427   if (is_inline_type()) {
4428     if (is_contended_class) {
4429       throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support @Contended annotation yet");
4430       return;
4431     }
4432   }
4433 
4434   // Compute the non-contended fields count.
4435   // The packing code below relies on these counts to determine if some field
4436   // can be squeezed into the alignment gap. Contended fields are obviously
4437   // exempt from that.
4438   unsigned int nonstatic_double_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE];
4439   unsigned int nonstatic_word_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_WORD];
4440   unsigned int nonstatic_short_count  = fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT]  - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_SHORT];
4441   unsigned int nonstatic_byte_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_BYTE];
4442   unsigned int nonstatic_oop_count    = fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP]    - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_OOP];
4443 
4444   int static_inline_type_count = 0;
4445   int nonstatic_inline_type_count = 0;
4446   int* nonstatic_inline_type_indexes = NULL;
4447   Klass** nonstatic_inline_type_klasses = NULL;
4448   unsigned int inline_type_oop_map_count = 0;
4449   int inline_types_not_inlined = 0;
4450   int not_atomic_inline_types = 0;
4451 
4452   int max_nonstatic_inline_type = fac->count[NONSTATIC_INLINE] + 1;
4453 
4454   nonstatic_inline_type_indexes = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, int,
4455                                                                max_nonstatic_inline_type);
4456   for (int i = 0; i < max_nonstatic_inline_type; i++) {
4457     nonstatic_inline_type_indexes[i] = -1;
4458   }
4459   nonstatic_inline_type_klasses = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, Klass*,
4460                                                                max_nonstatic_inline_type);
4461 
4462   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, _cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4463     if (fs.allocation_type() == STATIC_INLINE) {
4464       ResourceMark rm;
4465       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4466         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4467       }
4468       static_inline_type_count++;
4469     } else if (fs.allocation_type() == NONSTATIC_INLINE) {
4470       // Pre-resolve the inline field and check for inline type circularity issues.
4471       ResourceMark rm;
4472       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4473         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4474       }
4475       Klass* klass =
4476         SystemDictionary::resolve_inline_type_field_or_fail(&fs,
4477                                                             Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
4478                                                             _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
4479       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
4480       if (!klass->access_flags().is_inline_type()) {
4481         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError());
4482       }
4483       ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4484       // Conditions to apply flattening or not should be defined in a single place
4485       bool too_big_to_allocate_inline = (InlineFieldMaxFlatSize >= 0 &&
4486                                  (vk->size_helper() * HeapWordSize) > InlineFieldMaxFlatSize);
4487       bool too_atomic_to_allocate_inline = vk->is_declared_atomic();
4488       bool too_volatile_to_allocate_inline = fs.access_flags().is_volatile();
4489       if (vk->is_naturally_atomic()) {
4490         too_atomic_to_allocate_inline = false;
4491         // too_volatile_to_allocate_inline = false; //FIXME
4492         // volatile fields are currently never inlined, this could change in the future
4493       }
4494       if (!(too_big_to_allocate_inline | too_atomic_to_allocate_inline | too_volatile_to_allocate_inline)) {
4495         nonstatic_inline_type_indexes[nonstatic_inline_type_count] = fs.index();
4496         nonstatic_inline_type_klasses[nonstatic_inline_type_count] = klass;
4497         nonstatic_inline_type_count++;
4498 
4499         ValueKlass* vklass = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4500         if (vklass->contains_oops()) {
4501           inline_type_oop_map_count += vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4502         }
4503         fs.set_inlined(true);
4504         if (!vk->is_atomic()) {  // flat and non-atomic: take note
4505           not_atomic_inline_types++;
4506         }
4507       } else {
4508         inline_types_not_inlined++;
4509         fs.set_inlined(false);
4510       }
4511     }
4512   }
4513 
4514   // Adjusting non_static_oop_count to take into account inline types fields not inlined;
4515   nonstatic_oop_count += inline_types_not_inlined;
4516 
4517   // Total non-static fields count, including every contended field
4518   unsigned int nonstatic_fields_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD] +
4519                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE] +
4520                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_INLINE];
4521 
4522   const bool super_has_nonstatic_fields =
4523           (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_nonstatic_fields());
4524   const bool has_nonstatic_fields =
4525     super_has_nonstatic_fields || (nonstatic_fields_count != 0);
4526   const bool has_nonstatic_inline_fields = nonstatic_inline_type_count > 0;
4527 
4528   if (is_inline_type() && (!has_nonstatic_fields)) {
4529     // There are a number of fixes required throughout the type system and JIT
4530     throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support zero instance size yet");
4531     return;
4532   }
4533 
4534   // Prepare list of oops for oop map generation.
4535   //
4536   // "offset" and "count" lists are describing the set of contiguous oop
4537   // regions. offset[i] is the start of the i-th region, which then has
4538   // count[i] oops following. Before we know how many regions are required,
4539   // we pessimistically allocate the maps to fit all the oops into the
4540   // distinct regions.
4541   //
4542   int super_oop_map_count = (_super_klass == NULL) ? 0 :_super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4543   int max_oop_map_count =
4544       super_oop_map_count +
4545       fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] +
4546       inline_type_oop_map_count +
4547       inline_types_not_inlined;
4548 
4549   OopMapBlocksBuilder* nonstatic_oop_maps = new OopMapBlocksBuilder(max_oop_map_count);
4550   if (super_oop_map_count > 0) {
4551     nonstatic_oop_maps->initialize_inherited_blocks(_super_klass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps(),
4552                                                     _super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count());
4553   }
4554 
4555   int first_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0; // will be set for first oop field
4556 
4557   bool compact_fields  = true;
4558   bool allocate_oops_first = false;
4559 
4560   int next_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0;
4561   int next_nonstatic_double_offset = 0;
4562 
4563   // Rearrange fields for a given allocation style
4564   if (allocate_oops_first) {
4565     // Fields order: oops, longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, padded fields
4566     next_nonstatic_oop_offset    = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4567     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset +
4568                                     (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4569   } else {
4570     // Fields order: longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, oops, padded fields
4571     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4572   }
4573 
4574   int nonstatic_oop_space_count   = 0;
4575   int nonstatic_word_space_count  = 0;
4576   int nonstatic_short_space_count = 0;
4577   int nonstatic_byte_space_count  = 0;
4578   int nonstatic_oop_space_offset = 0;
4579   int nonstatic_word_space_offset = 0;
4580   int nonstatic_short_space_offset = 0;
4581   int nonstatic_byte_space_offset = 0;
4582 
4583   // Try to squeeze some of the fields into the gaps due to
4584   // long/double alignment.
4585   if (nonstatic_double_count > 0) {
4586     int offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4587     next_nonstatic_double_offset = align_up(offset, BytesPerLong);
4588     if (compact_fields && offset != next_nonstatic_double_offset) {
4589       // Allocate available fields into the gap before double field.
4590       int length = next_nonstatic_double_offset - offset;
4591       assert(length == BytesPerInt, "");
4592       nonstatic_word_space_offset = offset;
4593       if (nonstatic_word_count > 0) {
4594         nonstatic_word_count      -= 1;
4595         nonstatic_word_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4596         length -= BytesPerInt;
4597         offset += BytesPerInt;
4598       }
4599       nonstatic_short_space_offset = offset;
4600       while (length >= BytesPerShort && nonstatic_short_count > 0) {
4601         nonstatic_short_count       -= 1;
4602         nonstatic_short_space_count += 1;
4603         length -= BytesPerShort;
4604         offset += BytesPerShort;
4605       }
4606       nonstatic_byte_space_offset = offset;
4607       while (length > 0 && nonstatic_byte_count > 0) {
4608         nonstatic_byte_count       -= 1;
4609         nonstatic_byte_space_count += 1;
4610         length -= 1;
4611       }
4612       // Allocate oop field in the gap if there are no other fields for that.
4613       nonstatic_oop_space_offset = offset;
4614       if (length >= heapOopSize && nonstatic_oop_count > 0 &&
4615           !allocate_oops_first) { // when oop fields not first
4616         nonstatic_oop_count      -= 1;
4617         nonstatic_oop_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4618         length -= heapOopSize;
4619         offset += heapOopSize;
4620       }
4621     }
4622   }
4623 
4624   int next_nonstatic_word_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset +
4625                                      (nonstatic_double_count * BytesPerLong);
4626   int next_nonstatic_short_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset +
4627                                       (nonstatic_word_count * BytesPerInt);
4628   int next_nonstatic_byte_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset +
4629                                      (nonstatic_short_count * BytesPerShort);
4630   int next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset +
4631                                        nonstatic_byte_count;
4632 
4633   // let oops jump before padding with this allocation style
4634   if (!allocate_oops_first) {
4635     next_nonstatic_oop_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4636     if( nonstatic_oop_count > 0 ) {
4637       next_nonstatic_oop_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_oop_offset, heapOopSize);
4638     }
4639     next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset + (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4640   }
4641 
4642   // Aligning embedded inline types
4643   // bug below, the current algorithm to layout embedded inline types always put them at the
4644   // end of the layout, which doesn't match the different allocation policies the VM is
4645   // supposed to provide => FixMe
4646   // Note also that the current alignment policy is to make each inline type starting on a
4647   // 64 bits boundary. This could be optimized later. For instance, it could be nice to
4648   // align inline types according to their most constrained internal type.
4649   next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4650   int next_inline_type_index = 0;
4651 
4652   // Iterate over fields again and compute correct offsets.
4653   // The field allocation type was temporarily stored in the offset slot.
4654   // oop fields are located before non-oop fields (static and non-static).
4655   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4656 
4657     // skip already laid out fields
4658     if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4659 
4660     // contended instance fields are handled below
4661     if (fs.is_contended() && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4662 
4663     int real_offset = 0;
4664     const FieldAllocationType atype = (const FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4665 
4666     // pack the rest of the fields
4667     switch (atype) {
4668       // Inline types in static fields are handled with oops
4669       case STATIC_INLINE:   // Fallthrough
4670       case STATIC_OOP:
4671         real_offset = next_static_oop_offset;
4672         next_static_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4673         break;
4674       case STATIC_BYTE:
4675         real_offset = next_static_byte_offset;
4676         next_static_byte_offset += 1;
4677         break;
4678       case STATIC_SHORT:
4679         real_offset = next_static_short_offset;
4680         next_static_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4681         break;
4682       case STATIC_WORD:
4683         real_offset = next_static_word_offset;
4684         next_static_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4685         break;
4686       case STATIC_DOUBLE:
4687         real_offset = next_static_double_offset;
4688         next_static_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4689         break;
4690       case NONSTATIC_INLINE:
4691         if (fs.is_inlined()) {
4692           Klass* klass = nonstatic_inline_type_klasses[next_inline_type_index];
4693           assert(klass != NULL, "Klass should have been loaded and resolved earlier");
4694           assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(),"Must be an inline type");
4695           ValueKlass* vklass = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4696           real_offset = next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset;
4697           next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset += (vklass->size_helper()) * wordSize - vklass->first_field_offset();
4698           // aligning next inline type on a 64 bits boundary
4699           next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset, BytesPerLong);
4700           next_inline_type_index += 1;
4701 
4702           if (vklass->contains_oops()) { // add flatten oop maps
4703             int diff = real_offset - vklass->first_field_offset();
4704             const OopMapBlock* map = vklass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps();
4705             const OopMapBlock* const last_map = map + vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4706             while (map < last_map) {
4707               nonstatic_oop_maps->add(map->offset() + diff, map->count());
4708               map++;
4709             }
4710           }
4711           break;
4712         } else {
4713           // Fall through
4714         }
4715       case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4716         if( nonstatic_oop_space_count > 0 ) {
4717           real_offset = nonstatic_oop_space_offset;
4718           nonstatic_oop_space_offset += heapOopSize;
4719           nonstatic_oop_space_count  -= 1;
4720         } else {
4721           real_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset;
4722           next_nonstatic_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4723         }
4724         nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4725         break;
4726       case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4727         if( nonstatic_byte_space_count > 0 ) {
4728           real_offset = nonstatic_byte_space_offset;
4729           nonstatic_byte_space_offset += 1;
4730           nonstatic_byte_space_count  -= 1;
4731         } else {
4732           real_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset;
4733           next_nonstatic_byte_offset += 1;
4734         }
4735         break;
4736       case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4737         if( nonstatic_short_space_count > 0 ) {
4738           real_offset = nonstatic_short_space_offset;
4739           nonstatic_short_space_offset += BytesPerShort;
4740           nonstatic_short_space_count  -= 1;
4741         } else {
4742           real_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset;
4743           next_nonstatic_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4744         }
4745         break;
4746       case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4747         if( nonstatic_word_space_count > 0 ) {
4748           real_offset = nonstatic_word_space_offset;
4749           nonstatic_word_space_offset += BytesPerInt;
4750           nonstatic_word_space_count  -= 1;
4751         } else {
4752           real_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset;
4753           next_nonstatic_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4754         }
4755         break;
4756       case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4757         real_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4758         next_nonstatic_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4759         break;
4760       default:
4761         ShouldNotReachHere();
4762     }
4763     fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4764   }
4765 
4766 
4767   // Handle the contended cases.
4768   //
4769   // Each contended field should not intersect the cache line with another contended field.
4770   // In the absence of alignment information, we end up with pessimistically separating
4771   // the fields with full-width padding.
4772   //
4773   // Additionally, this should not break alignment for the fields, so we round the alignment up
4774   // for each field.
4775   if (nonstatic_contended_count > 0) {
4776 
4777     // if there is at least one contended field, we need to have pre-padding for them
4778     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4779 
4780     // collect all contended groups
4781     ResourceBitMap bm(cp->size());
4782     for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4783       // skip already laid out fields
4784       if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4785 
4786       if (fs.is_contended()) {
4787         bm.set_bit(fs.contended_group());
4788       }
4789     }
4790 
4791     int current_group = -1;
4792     while ((current_group = (int)bm.get_next_one_offset(current_group + 1)) != (int)bm.size()) {
4793 
4794       for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4795 
4796         // skip already laid out fields
4797         if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4798 
4799         // skip non-contended fields and fields from different group
4800         if (!fs.is_contended() || (fs.contended_group() != current_group)) continue;
4801 
4802         // handle statics below
4803         if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4804 
4805         int real_offset = 0;
4806         FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4807 
4808         switch (atype) {
4809           case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4810             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, 1);
4811             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4812             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += 1;
4813             break;
4814 
4815           case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4816             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerShort);
4817             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4818             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerShort;
4819             break;
4820 
4821           case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4822             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerInt);
4823             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4824             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerInt;
4825             break;
4826 
4827           case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4828             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4829             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4830             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerLong;
4831             break;
4832 
4833             // Inline types in static fields are handled with oops
4834           case NONSTATIC_INLINE:
4835             throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
4836                                       "@Contended annotation not supported for inline types yet", fs.name(), fs.signature());
4837             return;
4838 
4839           case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4840             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, heapOopSize);
4841             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4842             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += heapOopSize;
4843             nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4844             break;
4845 
4846           default:
4847             ShouldNotReachHere();
4848         }
4849 
4850         if (fs.contended_group() == 0) {
4851           // Contended group defines the equivalence class over the fields:
4852           // the fields within the same contended group are not inter-padded.
4853           // The only exception is default group, which does not incur the
4854           // equivalence, and so requires intra-padding.
4855           next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4856         }
4857 
4858         fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4859       } // for
4860 
4861       // Start laying out the next group.
4862       // Note that this will effectively pad the last group in the back;
4863       // this is expected to alleviate memory contention effects for
4864       // subclass fields and/or adjacent object.
4865       // If this was the default group, the padding is already in place.
4866       if (current_group != 0) {
4867         next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4868       }
4869     }
4870 
4871     // handle static fields
4872   }
4873 
4874   // Entire class is contended, pad in the back.
4875   // This helps to alleviate memory contention effects for subclass fields
4876   // and/or adjacent object.
4877   if (is_contended_class) {
4878     assert(!is_inline_type(), "@Contended not supported for inline types yet");
4879     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4880   }
4881 
4882   int notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end;
4883   if (nonstatic_inline_type_count != 0) {
4884     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_inline_type_offset;
4885   } else {
4886     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4887   }
4888 
4889   int nonstatic_field_sz_align = heapOopSize;
4890   if (is_inline_type()) {
4891     if ((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) > heapOopSize) {
4892       nonstatic_field_sz_align = BytesPerLong; // value copy of fields only uses jlong copy
4893     }
4894   }
4895   int nonstatic_fields_end      = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, nonstatic_field_sz_align);
4896   int instance_end              = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, wordSize);
4897   int static_fields_end         = align_up(next_static_byte_offset, wordSize);
4898 
4899   int static_field_size         = (static_fields_end -
4900                                    InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields()) / wordSize;
4901   nonstatic_field_size          = nonstatic_field_size +
4902                                   (nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) / heapOopSize;
4903 
4904   int instance_size             = align_object_size(instance_end / wordSize);
4905 
4906   assert(instance_size == align_object_size(align_up(
4907          (instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() + nonstatic_field_size*heapOopSize)
4908          + initial_inline_type_padding, wordSize) / wordSize), "consistent layout helper value");
4909 
4910 
4911   // Invariant: nonstatic_field end/start should only change if there are
4912   // nonstatic fields in the class, or if the class is contended. We compare
4913   // against the non-aligned value, so that end alignment will not fail the
4914   // assert without actually having the fields.
4915   assert((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end == nonstatic_fields_start) ||
4916          is_contended_class ||
4917          (nonstatic_fields_count > 0), "double-check nonstatic start/end");
4918 
4919   // Number of non-static oop map blocks allocated at end of klass.
4920   nonstatic_oop_maps->compact();
4921 
4922 #ifndef PRODUCT
4923   if ((PrintFieldLayout && !is_inline_type()) ||
4924       (PrintInlineLayout && (is_inline_type() || has_nonstatic_inline_fields))) {
4925     print_field_layout(_class_name,
4926           _fields,
4927           cp,
4928           instance_size,
4929           nonstatic_fields_start,
4930           nonstatic_fields_end,
4931           static_fields_end);
4932     nonstatic_oop_maps->print_on(tty);
4933     tty->print("\n");
4934     tty->print_cr("Instance size = %d", instance_size);
4935     tty->print_cr("Nonstatic_field_size = %d", nonstatic_field_size);
4936     tty->print_cr("Static_field_size = %d", static_field_size);
4937     tty->print_cr("Has nonstatic fields = %d", has_nonstatic_fields);
4938     tty->print_cr("---");
4939   }
4940 
4941 #endif
4942   // Pass back information needed for InstanceKlass creation
4943   info->oop_map_blocks = nonstatic_oop_maps;
4944   info->_instance_size = instance_size;
4945   info->_static_field_size = static_field_size;
4946   info->_nonstatic_field_size = nonstatic_field_size;
4947   info->_has_nonstatic_fields = has_nonstatic_fields;
4948   info->_has_inline_fields = nonstatic_inline_type_count > 0;
4949 
4950   // An inline type is naturally atomic if it has just one field, and
4951   // that field is simple enough.
4952   info->_is_naturally_atomic = (is_inline_type() &&
4953                                 !super_has_nonstatic_fields &&
4954                                 (nonstatic_fields_count <= 1) &&
4955                                 (not_atomic_inline_types == 0) &&
4956                                 (nonstatic_contended_count == 0));
4957   // This may be too restrictive, since if all the fields fit in 64
4958   // bits we could make the decision to align instances of this class
4959   // to 64-bit boundaries, and load and store them as single words.
4960   // And on machines which supported larger atomics we could similarly
4961   // allow larger values to be atomic, if properly aligned.
4962 }
4963 
4964 void ClassFileParser::set_precomputed_flags(InstanceKlass* ik) {
4965   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
4966 
4967   const Klass* const super = ik->super();
4968 
4969   // Check if this klass has an empty finalize method (i.e. one with return bytecode only),
4970   // in which case we don't have to register objects as finalizable
4971   if (!_has_empty_finalizer) {
4972     if (_has_finalizer ||
4973         (super != NULL && super->has_finalizer())) {
4974       ik->set_has_finalizer();
4975     }
4976   }
4977 
4978 #ifdef ASSERT
4979   bool f = false;
4980   const Method* const m = ik->lookup_method(vmSymbols::finalize_method_name(),
4981                                            vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
4982   if (m != NULL && !m->is_empty_method()) {
4983       f = true;
4984   }
4985 
4986   // Spec doesn't prevent agent from redefinition of empty finalizer.
4987   // Despite the fact that it's generally bad idea and redefined finalizer
4988   // will not work as expected we shouldn't abort vm in this case
4989   if (!ik->has_redefined_this_or_super()) {
4990     assert(ik->has_finalizer() == f, "inconsistent has_finalizer");
4991   }
4992 #endif
4993 
4994   // Check if this klass supports the java.lang.Cloneable interface
4995   if (SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass_loaded()) {
4996     if (ik->is_subtype_of(SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass())) {
4997       if (ik->is_value()) {
4998         Thread *THREAD = Thread::current();
4999         throwInlineTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support Cloneable");
5000         return;
5001       }
5002       ik->set_is_cloneable();
5003     }
5004   }
5005 
5006   // Check if this klass has a vanilla default constructor
5007   if (super == NULL) {
5008     // java.lang.Object has empty default constructor
5009     ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
5010   } else {
5011     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor() &&
5012         _has_vanilla_constructor) {
5013       ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
5014     }
5015 #ifdef ASSERT
5016     bool v = false;
5017     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor()) {
5018       const Method* const constructor =
5019         ik->find_method(vmSymbols::object_initializer_name(),
5020                        vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
5021       if (constructor != NULL && constructor->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
5022         v = true;
5023       }
5024     }
5025     assert(v == ik->has_vanilla_constructor(), "inconsistent has_vanilla_constructor");
5026 #endif
5027   }
5028 
5029   // If it cannot be fast-path allocated, set a bit in the layout helper.
5030   // See documentation of InstanceKlass::can_be_fastpath_allocated().
5031   assert(ik->size_helper() > 0, "layout_helper is initialized");
5032   if ((!RegisterFinalizersAtInit && ik->has_finalizer())
5033       || ik->is_abstract() || ik->is_interface()
5034       || (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Class() && ik->class_loader() == NULL)
5035       || ik->size_helper() >= FastAllocateSizeLimit) {
5036     // Forbid fast-path allocation.
5037     const jint lh = Klass::instance_layout_helper(ik->size_helper(), true);
5038     ik->set_layout_helper(lh);
5039   }
5040 }
5041 
5042 bool ClassFileParser::supports_inline_types() const {
5043   // Inline types are only supported by class file version 55 and later
5044   return _major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION;
5045 }
5046 
5047 // utility methods for appending an array with check for duplicates
5048 
5049 static void append_interfaces(GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* result,
5050                               const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const ifs) {
5051   // iterate over new interfaces
5052   for (int i = 0; i < ifs->length(); i++) {
5053     InstanceKlass* const e = ifs->at(i);
5054     assert(e->is_klass() && e->is_interface(), "just checking");
5055     // add new interface
5056     result->append_if_missing(e);
5057   }
5058 }
5059 
5060 static Array<InstanceKlass*>* compute_transitive_interfaces(const InstanceKlass* super,
5061                                                             Array<InstanceKlass*>* local_ifs,
5062                                                             ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
5063                                                             TRAPS) {
5064   assert(local_ifs != NULL, "invariant");
5065   assert(loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
5066 
5067   // Compute maximum size for transitive interfaces
5068   int max_transitive_size = 0;
5069   int super_size = 0;
5070   // Add superclass transitive interfaces size
5071   if (super != NULL) {
5072     super_size = super->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5073     max_transitive_size += super_size;
5074   }
5075   // Add local interfaces' super interfaces
5076   const int local_size = local_ifs->length();
5077   for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5078     InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5079     max_transitive_size += l->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5080   }
5081   // Finally add local interfaces
5082   max_transitive_size += local_size;
5083   // Construct array
5084   if (max_transitive_size == 0) {
5085     // no interfaces, use canonicalized array
5086     return Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
5087   } else if (max_transitive_size == super_size) {
5088     // no new local interfaces added, share superklass' transitive interface array
5089     return super->transitive_interfaces();
5090     // The three lines below are commented to work around bug JDK-8245487
5091 //  } else if (max_transitive_size == local_size) {
5092 //    // only local interfaces added, share local interface array
5093 //    return local_ifs;
5094   } else {
5095     ResourceMark rm;
5096     GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* const result = new GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>(max_transitive_size);
5097 
5098     // Copy down from superclass
5099     if (super != NULL) {
5100       append_interfaces(result, super->transitive_interfaces());
5101     }
5102 
5103     // Copy down from local interfaces' superinterfaces
5104     for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5105       InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5106       append_interfaces(result, l->transitive_interfaces());
5107     }
5108     // Finally add local interfaces
5109     append_interfaces(result, local_ifs);
5110 
5111     // length will be less than the max_transitive_size if duplicates were removed
5112     const int length = result->length();
5113     assert(length <= max_transitive_size, "just checking");
5114 
5115     if (length == 1 && result->at(0) == SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass()) {
5116       return Universe::the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array();
5117     }
5118 
5119     Array<InstanceKlass*>* const new_result =
