5120       MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(loader_data, length, CHECK_NULL);
5121     for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
5122       InstanceKlass* const e = result->at(i);
5123       assert(e != NULL, "just checking");
5124       new_result->at_put(i, e);
5125     }
5126     return new_result;
5127   }
5128 }
5129 
5130 static void check_super_class_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5131   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5132   const Klass* const super = this_klass->super();
5133 
5134   if (super != NULL) {
5135     const InstanceKlass* super_ik = InstanceKlass::cast(super);
5136 
5137     if (super->is_final()) {
5138       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5139       Exceptions::fthrow(
5140         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5141         vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5142         "class %s cannot inherit from final class %s",
5143         this_klass->external_name(),
5144         super_ik->external_name());
5145       return;
5146     }
5147 
5148     if (super_ik->is_sealed() && !super_ik->has_as_permitted_subclass(this_klass)) {
5149       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5150       Exceptions::fthrow(
5151         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5152         vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
5153         "class %s cannot inherit from sealed class %s",
5154         this_klass->external_name(),
5155         super_ik->external_name());
5156       return;
5157     }
5158 
5159     // If the loader is not the boot loader then throw an exception if its
5160     // superclass is in package jdk.internal.reflect and its loader is not a
5161     // special reflection class loader
5162     if (!this_klass->class_loader_data()->is_the_null_class_loader_data()) {
5163       PackageEntry* super_package = super->package();
5164       if (super_package != NULL &&
5165           super_package->name()->fast_compare(vmSymbols::jdk_internal_reflect()) == 0 &&
5166           !java_lang_ClassLoader::is_reflection_class_loader(this_klass->class_loader())) {
5167         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5168         Exceptions::fthrow(
5169           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5170           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5171           "class %s loaded by %s cannot access jdk/internal/reflect superclass %s",
5172           this_klass->external_name(),
5173           this_klass->class_loader_data()->loader_name_and_id(),
5174           super->external_name());
5175         return;
5176       }
5177     }
5178 
5179     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5180       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, InstanceKlass::cast(super), false);
5181     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5182       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5183       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5184                                                       InstanceKlass::cast(super),
5185                                                       vca_result);
5186       if (msg == NULL) {
5187         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == super->module());
5188         Exceptions::fthrow(
5189           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5190           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5191           "class %s cannot access its %ssuperclass %s (%s%s%s)",
5192           this_klass->external_name(),
5193           super->is_abstract() ? "abstract " : "",
5194           super->external_name(),
5195           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(super) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5196           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5197           (same_module) ? "" : super->class_in_module_of_loader());
5198       } else {
5199         // Add additional message content.
5200         Exceptions::fthrow(
5201           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5202           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5203           "superclass access check failed: %s",
5204           msg);
5205       }
5206     }
5207   }
5208 }
5209 
5210 
5211 static void check_super_interface_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5212   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5213   const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = this_klass->local_interfaces();
5214   const int lng = local_interfaces->length();
5215   for (int i = lng - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
5216     InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
5217     assert (k != NULL && k->is_interface(), "invalid interface");
5218 
5219     if (k->is_sealed() && !k->has_as_permitted_subclass(this_klass)) {
5220       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5221       Exceptions::fthrow(
5222         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5223         vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
5224         "class %s cannot %s sealed interface %s",
5225         this_klass->external_name(),
5226         this_klass->is_interface() ? "extend" : "implement",
5227         k->external_name());
5228       return;
5229     }
5230 
5231     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5232       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, k, false);
5233     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5234       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5235       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5236                                                       k,
5237                                                       vca_result);
5238       if (msg == NULL) {
5239         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == k->module());
5240         Exceptions::fthrow(
5241           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5242           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5243           "class %s cannot access its superinterface %s (%s%s%s)",
5244           this_klass->external_name(),
5245           k->external_name(),
5246           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(k) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5247           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5248           (same_module) ? "" : k->class_in_module_of_loader());
5249       } else {
5250         // Add additional message content.
5251         Exceptions::fthrow(
5252           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5253           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5254           "superinterface check failed: %s",
5255           msg);
5256       }
5257     }
5258   }
5259 }
5260 
5261 
5262 static void check_final_method_override(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5263   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5264   const Array<Method*>* const methods = this_klass->methods();
5265   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5266 
5267   // go thru each method and check if it overrides a final method
5268   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5269     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5270 
5271     // skip private, static, and <init> methods
5272     if ((!m->is_private() && !m->is_static()) &&
5273         (m->name() != vmSymbols::object_initializer_name())) {
5274 
5275       const Symbol* const name = m->name();
5276       const Symbol* const signature = m->signature();
5277       const Klass* k = this_klass->super();
5278       const Method* super_m = NULL;
5279       while (k != NULL) {
5280         // skip supers that don't have final methods.
5281         if (k->has_final_method()) {
5282           // lookup a matching method in the super class hierarchy
5283           super_m = InstanceKlass::cast(k)->lookup_method(name, signature);
5284           if (super_m == NULL) {
5285             break; // didn't find any match; get out
5286           }
5287 
5288           if (super_m->is_final() && !super_m->is_static() &&
5289               !super_m->access_flags().is_private()) {
5290             // matching method in super is final, and not static or private
5291             bool can_access = Reflection::verify_member_access(this_klass,
5292                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5293                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5294                                                                super_m->access_flags(),
5295                                                               false, false, CHECK);
5296             if (can_access) {
5297               // this class can access super final method and therefore override
5298               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5299               Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5300                                  vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5301                                  "class %s overrides final method %s.%s%s",
5302                                  this_klass->external_name(),
5303                                  super_m->method_holder()->external_name(),
5304                                  name->as_C_string(),
5305                                  signature->as_C_string()
5306                                  );
5307               return;
5308             }
5309           }
5310 
5311           // continue to look from super_m's holder's super.
5312           k = super_m->method_holder()->super();
5313           continue;
5314         }
5315 
5316         k = k->super();
5317       }
5318     }
5319   }
5320 }
5321 
5322 
5323 // assumes that this_klass is an interface
5324 static void check_illegal_static_method(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5325   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5326   assert(this_klass->is_interface(), "not an interface");
5327   const Array<Method*>* methods = this_klass->methods();
5328   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5329 
5330   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5331     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5332     // if m is static and not the init method, throw a verify error
5333     if ((m->is_static()) && (m->name() != vmSymbols::class_initializer_name())) {
5334       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5335       Exceptions::fthrow(
5336         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5337         vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5338         "Illegal static method %s in interface %s",
5339         m->name()->as_C_string(),
5340         this_klass->external_name()
5341       );
5342       return;
5343     }
5344   }
5345 }
5346 
5347 // utility methods for format checking
5348 
5349 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_modifiers(jint flags, TRAPS) const {
5350   const bool is_module = (flags & JVM_ACC_MODULE) != 0;
5351   const bool is_inline_type = (flags & JVM_ACC_VALUE) != 0;
5352   assert(_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION || !is_module, "JVM_ACC_MODULE should not be set");
5353   assert(supports_inline_types() || !is_inline_type, "JVM_ACC_VALUE should not be set");
5354   if (is_module) {
5355     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5356     Exceptions::fthrow(
5357       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5358       vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
5359       "%s is not a class because access_flag ACC_MODULE is set",
5360       _class_name->as_C_string());
5361     return;
5362   }
5363 
5364   if (is_inline_type && !EnableValhalla) {
5365     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5366     Exceptions::fthrow(
5367       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5368       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5369       "Class modifier ACC_VALUE in class %s requires option -XX:+EnableValhalla",
5370       _class_name->as_C_string()
5371     );
5372   }
5373 
5374   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5375 
5376   const bool is_interface  = (flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE)  != 0;
5377   const bool is_abstract   = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)   != 0;
5378   const bool is_final      = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)      != 0;
5379   const bool is_super      = (flags & JVM_ACC_SUPER)      != 0;
5380   const bool is_enum       = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)       != 0;
5381   const bool is_annotation = (flags & JVM_ACC_ANNOTATION) != 0;
5382   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5383   const bool major_gte_14  = _major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION;
5384 
5385   if ((is_abstract && is_final) ||
5386       (is_interface && !is_abstract) ||
5387       (is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && (is_super || is_enum)) ||
5388       (!is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && is_annotation) ||
5389       (is_inline_type && (is_interface || is_abstract || is_enum || !is_final))) {
5390     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5391     const char* class_note = "";
5392     if (is_inline_type)  class_note = " (an inline class)";
5393     Exceptions::fthrow(
5394       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5395       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5396       "Illegal class modifiers in class %s%s: 0x%X",
5397       _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags
5398     );
5399     return;
5400   }
5401 }
5402 
5403 static bool has_illegal_visibility(jint flags) {
5404   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5405   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5406   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5407 
5408   return ((is_public && is_protected) ||
5409           (is_public && is_private) ||
5410           (is_protected && is_private));
5411 }
5412 
5413 // A legal major_version.minor_version must be one of the following:
5414 //
5415 //  Major_version >= 45 and major_version < 56, any minor_version.
5416 //  Major_version >= 56 and major_version <= JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 0.
5417 //  Major_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 65535 and --enable-preview is present.
5418 //
5419 static void verify_class_version(u2 major, u2 minor, Symbol* class_name, TRAPS){
5420   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5421   const u2 max_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION;
5422   if (major < JAVA_MIN_SUPPORTED_VERSION) {
5423     Exceptions::fthrow(
5424       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5425       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5426       "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid major version",
5427       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5428     return;
5429   }
5430 
5431   if (major > max_version) {
5432     Exceptions::fthrow(
5433       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5434       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5435       "%s has been compiled by a more recent version of the Java Runtime (class file version %u.%u), "
5436       "this version of the Java Runtime only recognizes class file versions up to %u.0",
5437       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
5438     return;
5439   }
5440 
5441   if (major < JAVA_12_VERSION || minor == 0) {
5442     return;
5443   }
5444 
5445   if (minor == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION) {
5446     if (major != max_version) {
5447       Exceptions::fthrow(
5448         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5449         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5450         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with preview features that are unsupported. "
5451         "This version of the Java Runtime only recognizes preview features for class file version %u.%u",
5452         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION, JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION);
5453       return;
5454     }
5455 
5456     if (!Arguments::enable_preview()) {
5457       Exceptions::fthrow(
5458         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5459         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5460         "Preview features are not enabled for %s (class file version %u.%u). Try running with '--enable-preview'",
5461         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5462       return;
5463     }
5464 
5465   } else { // minor != JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION
5466     Exceptions::fthrow(
5467         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5468         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5469         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid non-zero minor version",
5470         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5471   }
5472 }
5473 
5474 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_modifiers(jint flags,
5475                                                    bool is_interface,
5476                                                    bool is_inline_type,
5477                                                    TRAPS) const {
5478   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5479 
5480   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5481   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5482   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5483   const bool is_static    = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)    != 0;
5484   const bool is_final     = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)     != 0;
5485   const bool is_volatile  = (flags & JVM_ACC_VOLATILE)  != 0;
5486   const bool is_transient = (flags & JVM_ACC_TRANSIENT) != 0;
5487   const bool is_enum      = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)      != 0;
5488   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5489 
5490   bool is_illegal = false;
5491 
5492   if (is_interface) {
5493     if (!is_public || !is_static || !is_final || is_private ||
5494         is_protected || is_volatile || is_transient ||
5495         (major_gte_1_5 && is_enum)) {
5496       is_illegal = true;
5497     }
5498   } else { // not interface
5499     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags) || (is_final && is_volatile)) {
5500       is_illegal = true;
5501     } else {
5502       if (is_inline_type && !is_static && !is_final) {
5503         is_illegal = true;
5504       }
5505     }
5506   }
5507 
5508   if (is_illegal) {
5509     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5510     Exceptions::fthrow(
5511       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5512       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5513       "Illegal field modifiers in class %s: 0x%X",
5514       _class_name->as_C_string(), flags);
5515     return;
5516   }
5517 }
5518 
5519 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_modifiers(jint flags,
5520                                                     bool is_interface,
5521                                                     bool is_inline_type,
5522                                                     const Symbol* name,
5523                                                     TRAPS) const {
5524   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5525 
5526   const bool is_public       = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)       != 0;
5527   const bool is_private      = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)      != 0;
5528   const bool is_static       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)       != 0;
5529   const bool is_final        = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)        != 0;
5530   const bool is_native       = (flags & JVM_ACC_NATIVE)       != 0;
5531   const bool is_abstract     = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)     != 0;
5532   const bool is_bridge       = (flags & JVM_ACC_BRIDGE)       != 0;
5533   const bool is_strict       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STRICT)       != 0;
5534   const bool is_synchronized = (flags & JVM_ACC_SYNCHRONIZED) != 0;
5535   const bool is_protected    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED)    != 0;
5536   const bool major_gte_1_5   = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5537   const bool major_gte_8     = _major_version >= JAVA_8_VERSION;
5538   const bool is_initializer  = (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name());
5539 
5540   bool is_illegal = false;
5541 
5542   const char* class_note = "";
5543 
5544   if (is_interface) {
5545     if (major_gte_8) {
5546       // Class file version is JAVA_8_VERSION or later Methods of
5547       // interfaces may set any of the flags except ACC_PROTECTED,
5548       // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, and ACC_SYNCHRONIZED; they must
5549       // have exactly one of the ACC_PUBLIC or ACC_PRIVATE flags set.
5550       if ((is_public == is_private) || /* Only one of private and public should be true - XNOR */
5551           (is_native || is_protected || is_final || is_synchronized) ||
5552           // If a specific method of a class or interface has its
5553           // ACC_ABSTRACT flag set, it must not have any of its
5554           // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, ACC_PRIVATE, ACC_STATIC,
5555           // ACC_STRICT, or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED flags set.  No need to
5556           // check for ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED as
5557           // those flags are illegal irrespective of ACC_ABSTRACT being set or not.
5558           (is_abstract && (is_private || is_static || is_strict))) {
5559         is_illegal = true;
5560       }
5561     } else if (major_gte_1_5) {
5562       // Class file version in the interval [JAVA_1_5_VERSION, JAVA_8_VERSION)
5563       if (!is_public || is_private || is_protected || is_static || is_final ||
5564           is_synchronized || is_native || !is_abstract || is_strict) {
5565         is_illegal = true;
5566       }
5567     } else {
5568       // Class file version is pre-JAVA_1_5_VERSION
5569       if (!is_public || is_static || is_final || is_native || !is_abstract) {
5570         is_illegal = true;
5571       }
5572     }
5573   } else { // not interface
5574     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags)) {
5575       is_illegal = true;
5576     } else {
5577       if (is_initializer) {
5578         if (is_final || is_synchronized || is_native ||
5579             is_abstract || (major_gte_1_5 && is_bridge)) {
5580           is_illegal = true;
5581         }
5582         if (!is_static && !is_inline_type) {
5583           // OK, an object constructor in a regular class
5584         } else if (is_static && is_inline_type) {
5585           // OK, a static init factory in an inline class
5586         } else {
5587           // but no other combinations are allowed
5588           is_illegal = true;
5589           class_note = (is_inline_type ? " (an inline class)" : " (not an inline class)");
5590         }
5591       } else { // not initializer
5592         if (is_inline_type && is_synchronized && !is_static) {
5593           is_illegal = true;
5594           class_note = " (an inline class)";
5595         } else {
5596           if (is_abstract) {
5597             if ((is_final || is_native || is_private || is_static ||
5598                 (major_gte_1_5 && (is_synchronized || is_strict)))) {
5599               is_illegal = true;
5600             }
5601           }
5602         }
5603       }
5604     }
5605   }
5606 
5607   if (is_illegal) {
5608     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5609     Exceptions::fthrow(
5610       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5611       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5612       "Method %s in class %s%s has illegal modifiers: 0x%X",
5613       name->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags);
5614     return;
5615   }
5616 }
5617 
5618 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_utf8(const unsigned char* buffer,
5619                                         int length,
5620                                         TRAPS) const {
5621   assert(_need_verify, "only called when _need_verify is true");
5622   if (!UTF8::is_legal_utf8(buffer, length, _major_version <= 47)) {
5623     classfile_parse_error("Illegal UTF8 string in constant pool in class file %s", CHECK);
5624   }
5625 }
5626 
5627 // Unqualified names may not contain the characters '.', ';', '[', or '/'.
5628 // In class names, '/' separates unqualified names.  This is verified in this function also.
5629 // Method names also may not contain the characters '<' or '>', unless <init>
5630 // or <clinit>.  Note that method names may not be <init> or <clinit> in this
5631 // method.  Because these names have been checked as special cases before
5632 // calling this method in verify_legal_method_name.
5633 //
5634 // This method is also called from the modular system APIs in modules.cpp
5635 // to verify the validity of module and package names.
5636 bool ClassFileParser::verify_unqualified_name(const char* name,
5637                                               unsigned int length,
5638                                               int type) {
5639   if (length == 0) return false;  // Must have at least one char.
5640   for (const char* p = name; p != name + length; p++) {
5641     switch(*p) {
5642       case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT:
5643       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS:
5644       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5645         // do not permit '.', ';', or '['
5646         return false;
5647       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH:
5648         // check for '//' or leading or trailing '/' which are not legal
5649         // unqualified name must not be empty
5650         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalClass) {
5651           if (p == name || p+1 >= name+length ||
5652               *(p+1) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5653             return false;
5654           }
5655         } else {
5656           return false;   // do not permit '/' unless it's class name
5657         }
5658         break;
5659       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL:
5660       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDSPECIAL:
5661         // do not permit '<' or '>' in method names
5662         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalMethod) {
5663           return false;
5664         }
5665     }
5666   }
5667   return true;
5668 }
5669 
5670 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5671 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5672 // be taken as a fieldname. Allow '/' if slash_ok is true.
5673 // Return a pointer to just past the fieldname.
5674 // Return NULL if no fieldname at all was found, or in the case of slash_ok
5675 // being true, we saw consecutive slashes (meaning we were looking for a
5676 // qualified path but found something that was badly-formed).
5677 static const char* skip_over_field_name(const char* const name,
5678                                         bool slash_ok,
5679                                         unsigned int length) {
5680   const char* p;
5681   jboolean last_is_slash = false;
5682   jboolean not_first_ch = false;
5683 
5684   for (p = name; p != name + length; not_first_ch = true) {
5685     const char* old_p = p;
5686     jchar ch = *p;
5687     if (ch < 128) {
5688       p++;
5689       // quick check for ascii
5690       if ((ch >= 'a' && ch <= 'z') ||
5691         (ch >= 'A' && ch <= 'Z') ||
5692         (ch == '_' || ch == '$') ||
5693         (not_first_ch && ch >= '0' && ch <= '9')) {
5694         last_is_slash = false;
5695         continue;
5696       }
5697       if (slash_ok && ch == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5698         if (last_is_slash) {
5699           return NULL;  // Don't permit consecutive slashes
5700         }
5701         last_is_slash = true;
5702         continue;
5703       }
5704     }
5705     else {
5706       jint unicode_ch;
5707       char* tmp_p = UTF8::next_character(p, &unicode_ch);
5708       p = tmp_p;
5709       last_is_slash = false;
5710       // Check if ch is Java identifier start or is Java identifier part
5711       // 4672820: call java.lang.Character methods directly without generating separate tables.
5712       EXCEPTION_MARK;
5713       // return value
5714       JavaValue result(T_BOOLEAN);
5715       // Set up the arguments to isJavaIdentifierStart or isJavaIdentifierPart
5716       JavaCallArguments args;
5717       args.push_int(unicode_ch);
5718 
5719       if (not_first_ch) {
5720         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierPart(char ch);
5721         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5722           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5723           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierPart_name(),
5724           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5725           &args,
5726           THREAD);
5727       } else {
5728         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierStart(char ch);
5729         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5730           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5731           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierStart_name(),
5732           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5733           &args,
5734           THREAD);
5735       }
5736       if (HAS_PENDING_EXCEPTION) {
5737         CLEAR_PENDING_EXCEPTION;
5738         return NULL;
5739       }
5740       if(result.get_jboolean()) {
5741         continue;
5742       }
5743     }
5744     return (not_first_ch) ? old_p : NULL;
5745   }
5746   return (not_first_ch) ? p : NULL;
5747 }
5748 
5749 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5750 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5751 // be taken as a field signature. Allow "void" if void_ok.
5752 // Return a pointer to just past the signature.
5753 // Return NULL if no legal signature is found.
5754 const char* ClassFileParser::skip_over_field_signature(const char* signature,
5755                                                        bool void_ok,
5756                                                        unsigned int length,
5757                                                        TRAPS) const {
5758   unsigned int array_dim = 0;
5759   while (length > 0) {
5760     switch (signature[0]) {
5761     case JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID: if (!void_ok) { return NULL; }
5762     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BOOLEAN:
5763     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BYTE:
5764     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CHAR:
5765     case JVM_SIGNATURE_SHORT:
5766     case JVM_SIGNATURE_INT:
5767     case JVM_SIGNATURE_FLOAT:
5768     case JVM_SIGNATURE_LONG:
5769     case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOUBLE:
5770       return signature + 1;
5771     case JVM_SIGNATURE_INLINE_TYPE:
5772       // Can't enable this check until JDK upgrades the bytecode generators
5773       // if (_major_version < CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS ) {
5774       //   classfile_parse_error("Class name contains illegal Q-signature "
5775       //                                    "in descriptor in class file %s",
5776       //                                    CHECK_0);
5777       // }
5778       // fall through
5779     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CLASS:
5780     {
5781       if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5782         // Skip over the class name if one is there
5783         const char* const p = skip_over_field_name(signature + 1, true, --length);
5784 
5785         // The next character better be a semicolon
5786         if (p && (p - signature) > 1 && p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS) {
5787           return p + 1;
5788         }
5789       }
5790       else {
5791         // Skip leading 'L' or 'Q' and ignore first appearance of ';'
5792         signature++;
5793         const char* c = (const char*) memchr(signature, JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS, length - 1);
5794         // Format check signature
5795         if (c != NULL) {
5796           int newlen = c - (char*) signature;
5797           bool legal = verify_unqualified_name(signature, newlen, LegalClass);
5798           if (!legal) {
5799             classfile_parse_error("Class name is empty or contains illegal character "
5800                                   "in descriptor in class file %s",
5801                                   CHECK_NULL);
5802             return NULL;
5803           }
5804           return signature + newlen + 1;
5805         }
5806       }
5807       return NULL;
5808     }
5809     case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5810       array_dim++;
5811       if (array_dim > 255) {
5812         // 4277370: array descriptor is valid only if it represents 255 or fewer dimensions.
5813         classfile_parse_error("Array type descriptor has more than 255 dimensions in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
5814       }
5815       // The rest of what's there better be a legal signature
5816       signature++;
5817       length--;
5818       void_ok = false;
5819       break;
5820     default:
5821       return NULL;
5822     }
5823   }
5824   return NULL;
5825 }
5826 
5827 // Checks if name is a legal class name.
5828 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5829   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5830 
5831   assert(name->refcount() > 0, "symbol must be kept alive");
5832   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5833   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5834   bool legal = false;
5835 
5836   if (length > 0) {
5837     const char* p;
5838     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY) {
5839       p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5840       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5841     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5842       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5843         p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, true, length);
5844         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5845       }
5846     } else if (_major_version >= CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS && bytes[length - 1] == ';' ) {
5847       // Support for L...; and Q...; descriptors
5848       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes + 1, length - 2, LegalClass);
5849     } else {
5850       // 4900761: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5851       // Class names may be drawn from the entire Unicode character set.
5852       // Identifiers between '/' must be unqualified names.
5853       // The utf8 string has been verified when parsing cpool entries.
5854       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalClass);
5855     }
5856   }
5857   if (!legal) {
5858     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5859     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5860     Exceptions::fthrow(
5861       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5862       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5863       "Illegal class name \"%.*s\" in class file %s", length, bytes,
5864       _class_name->as_C_string()
5865     );
5866     return;
5867   }
5868 }
5869 
5870 // Checks if name is a legal field name.
5871 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5872   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5873 
5874   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5875   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5876   bool legal = false;
5877 
5878   if (length > 0) {
5879     if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5880       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5881         const char* p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5882         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5883       }
5884     } else {
5885       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5886       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalField);
5887     }
5888   }
5889 
5890   if (!legal) {
5891     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5892     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5893     Exceptions::fthrow(
5894       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5895       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5896       "Illegal field name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5897       _class_name->as_C_string()
5898     );
5899     return;
5900   }
5901 }
5902 
5903 // Checks if name is a legal method name.
5904 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5905   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5906 
5907   assert(name != NULL, "method name is null");
5908   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5909   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5910   bool legal = false;
5911 
5912   if (length > 0) {
5913     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5914       if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name() || name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name()) {
5915         legal = true;
5916       }
5917     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5918       const char* p;
5919       p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5920       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5921     } else {
5922       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5923       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalMethod);
5924     }
5925   }
5926 
5927   if (!legal) {
5928     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5929     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5930     Exceptions::fthrow(
5931       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5932       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5933       "Illegal method name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5934       _class_name->as_C_string()
5935     );
5936     return;
5937   }
5938 }
5939 
5940 
5941 // Checks if signature is a legal field signature.
5942 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_signature(const Symbol* name,
5943                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5944                                                    TRAPS) const {
5945   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5946 
5947   const char* const bytes = (const char* const)signature->bytes();
5948   const unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5949   const char* const p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5950 
5951   if (p == NULL || (p - bytes) != (int)length) {
5952     throwIllegalSignature("Field", name, signature, CHECK);
5953   }
5954 }
5955 
5956 // Checks if signature is a legal method signature.
5957 // Returns number of parameters
5958 int ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_signature(const Symbol* name,
5959                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5960                                                    TRAPS) const {
5961   if (!_need_verify) {
5962     // make sure caller's args_size will be less than 0 even for non-static
5963     // method so it will be recomputed in compute_size_of_parameters().
5964     return -2;
5965   }
5966 
5967   // Class initializers cannot have args for class format version >= 51.
5968   if (name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name() &&
5969       signature != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() &&
5970       _major_version >= JAVA_7_VERSION) {
5971     throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
5972     return 0;
5973   }
5974 
5975   unsigned int args_size = 0;
5976   const char* p = (const char*)signature->bytes();
5977   unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5978   const char* nextp;
5979 
5980   // The first character must be a '('
5981   if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_FUNC)) {
5982     length--;
5983     // Skip over legal field signatures
5984     nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5985     while ((length > 0) && (nextp != NULL)) {
5986       args_size++;
5987       if (p[0] == 'J' || p[0] == 'D') {
5988         args_size++;
5989       }
5990       length -= nextp - p;
5991       p = nextp;
5992       nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5993     }
5994     // The first non-signature thing better be a ')'
5995     if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDFUNC)) {
5996       length--;
5997       if (name->utf8_length() > 0 && name->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5998         // All constructor methods must return void
5999         if ((length == 1) && (p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID)) {
6000           return args_size;
6001         }
6002         // All static init methods must return the current class
6003         if ((length >= 3) && (p[length-1] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS)
6004             && name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
6005           nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
6006           if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
6007             // The actual class will be checked against current class
6008             // when the method is defined (see parse_method).
6009             // A reference to a static init with a bad return type
6010             // will load and verify OK, but will fail to link.
6011             return args_size;
6012           }
6013         }
6014         // The distinction between static factory methods and
6015         // constructors depends on the JVM_ACC_STATIC modifier.
6016         // This distinction must be reflected in a void or non-void
6017         // return. For declared methods, the check is in parse_method.
6018       } else {
6019         // Now we better just have a return value
6020         nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
6021         if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
6022           return args_size;
6023         }
6024       }
6025     }
6026   }
6027   // Report error
6028   throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
6029   return 0;
6030 }
6031 
6032 int ClassFileParser::static_field_size() const {
6033   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6034   return _field_info->_static_field_size;
6035 }
6036 
6037 int ClassFileParser::total_oop_map_count() const {
6038   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6039   return _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count;
6040 }
6041 
6042 jint ClassFileParser::layout_size() const {
6043   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6044   return _field_info->_instance_size;
6045 }
6046 
6047 static void check_methods_for_intrinsics(const InstanceKlass* ik,
6048                                          const Array<Method*>* methods) {
6049   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
6050   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
6051 
6052   // Set up Method*::intrinsic_id as soon as we know the names of methods.
6053   // (We used to do this lazily, but now we query it in Rewriter,
6054   // which is eagerly done for every method, so we might as well do it now,
6055   // when everything is fresh in memory.)
6056   const vmSymbols::SID klass_id = Method::klass_id_for_intrinsics(ik);
6057 
6058   if (klass_id != vmSymbols::NO_SID) {
6059     for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
6060       Method* method = methods->at(j);
6061       method->init_intrinsic_id();
6062 
6063       if (CheckIntrinsics) {
6064         // Check if an intrinsic is defined for method 'method',
6065         // but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.
6066         if (method->intrinsic_id() != vmIntrinsics::_none &&
6067             !method->intrinsic_candidate()) {
6068               tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
6069               "but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.%s",
6070               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
6071               NOT_DEBUG(" Method will not be inlined.") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6072             );
6073           tty->cr();
6074           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6075         }
6076         // Check is the method 'method' is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate,
6077         // but there is no intrinsic available for it.
6078         if (method->intrinsic_candidate() &&
6079           method->intrinsic_id() == vmIntrinsics::_none) {
6080             tty->print("Method [%s] is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate, "
6081               "but no compiler intrinsic is defined for the method.%s",
6082               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
6083               NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6084             );
6085           tty->cr();
6086           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6087         }
6088       }
6089     } // end for
6090 
6091 #ifdef ASSERT
6092     if (CheckIntrinsics) {
6093       // Check for orphan methods in the current class. A method m
6094       // of a class C is orphan if an intrinsic is defined for method m,
6095       // but class C does not declare m.
6096       // The check is potentially expensive, therefore it is available
6097       // only in debug builds.
6098 
6099       for (int id = vmIntrinsics::FIRST_ID; id < (int)vmIntrinsics::ID_LIMIT; ++id) {
6100         if (vmIntrinsics::_compiledLambdaForm == id) {
6101           // The _compiledLamdbdaForm intrinsic is a special marker for bytecode
6102           // generated for the JVM from a LambdaForm and therefore no method
6103           // is defined for it.
6104           continue;
6105         }
6106 
6107         if (vmIntrinsics::class_for(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id)) == klass_id) {
6108           // Check if the current class contains a method with the same
6109           // name, flags, signature.
6110           bool match = false;
6111           for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
6112             const Method* method = methods->at(j);
6113             if (method->intrinsic_id() == id) {
6114               match = true;
6115               break;
6116             }
6117           }
6118 
6119           if (!match) {
6120             char buf[1000];
6121             tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
6122                        "but the method is not available in class [%s].%s",
6123                         vmIntrinsics::short_name_as_C_string(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id),
6124                                                              buf, sizeof(buf)),
6125                         ik->name()->as_C_string(),
6126                         NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6127             );
6128             tty->cr();
6129             DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6130           }
6131         }
6132       } // end for
6133     } // CheckIntrinsics
6134 #endif // ASSERT
6135   }
6136 }
6137 
6138 InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::create_instance_klass(bool changed_by_loadhook,
6139                                                       const ClassInstanceInfo& cl_inst_info,
6140                                                       TRAPS) {
6141   if (_klass != NULL) {
6142     return _klass;
6143   }
6144 
6145   InstanceKlass* const ik =
6146     InstanceKlass::allocate_instance_klass(*this, CHECK_NULL);
6147 
6148   if (is_hidden()) {
6149     mangle_hidden_class_name(ik);
6150   }
6151 
6152   fill_instance_klass(ik, changed_by_loadhook, cl_inst_info, CHECK_NULL);
6153 
6154   assert(_klass == ik, "invariant");
6155 
6156 
6157   if (ik->should_store_fingerprint()) {
6158     ik->store_fingerprint(_stream->compute_fingerprint());
6159   }
6160 
6161   ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(false);
6162   if (UseAOT && ik->supers_have_passed_fingerprint_checks()) {
6163     uint64_t aot_fp = AOTLoader::get_saved_fingerprint(ik);
6164     uint64_t fp = ik->has_stored_fingerprint() ? ik->get_stored_fingerprint() : _stream->compute_fingerprint();
6165     if (aot_fp != 0 && aot_fp == fp) {
6166       // This class matches with a class saved in an AOT library
6167       ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(true);
6168     } else {
6169       ResourceMark rm;
6170       log_info(class, fingerprint)("%s :  expected = " PTR64_FORMAT " actual = " PTR64_FORMAT,
6171                                  ik->external_name(), aot_fp, _stream->compute_fingerprint());
6172     }
6173   }
6174 
6175   if (ik->is_value()) {
6176     ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(ik);
6177     oop val = ik->allocate_instance(CHECK_NULL);
6178     vk->set_default_value(val);
6179   }
6180 
6181   return ik;
6182 }
6183 
6184 // Return true if the specified class is not a valid super class for an inline type.
6185 // A valid super class for an inline type is abstract, has no instance fields,
6186 // does not implement interface java.lang.IdentityObject (checked elsewhere), has
6187 // an empty body-less no-arg constructor, and no synchronized instance methods.
6188 // This function doesn't check if the class's super types are invalid.  Those checks
6189 // are done elsewhere.  The final determination of whether or not a class is an
6190 // invalid super type for an inline class is done in fill_instance_klass().
6191 bool ClassFileParser::is_invalid_super_for_inline_type() {
6192   if (class_name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6193     return true;
6194   }
6195   if (is_interface() || class_name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
6196     return false;
6197   }
6198   if (!access_flags().is_abstract() || _has_nonstatic_fields) {
6199     return true;
6200   } else {
6201     // Look at each method
6202     for (int x = 0; x < _methods->length(); x++) {
6203       const Method* const method = _methods->at(x);
6204       if (method->is_synchronized() && !method->is_static()) {
6205         return true;
6206 
6207       } else if (method->name() == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
6208         if (method->signature() != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() ||
6209             !method->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
6210           return true;
6211         }
6212       }
6213     }
6214   }
6215   return false;
6216 }
6217 
6218 void ClassFileParser::fill_instance_klass(InstanceKlass* ik,
6219                                           bool changed_by_loadhook,
6220                                           const ClassInstanceInfo& cl_inst_info,
6221                                           TRAPS) {
6222   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
6223 
6224   // Set name and CLD before adding to CLD
6225   ik->set_class_loader_data(_loader_data);
6226   ik->set_name(_class_name);
6227 
6228   // Add all classes to our internal class loader list here,
6229   // including classes in the bootstrap (NULL) class loader.
6230   const bool publicize = !is_internal();
6231 
6232   _loader_data->add_class(ik, publicize);
6233 
6234   set_klass_to_deallocate(ik);
6235 
6236   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6237   assert(ik->static_field_size() == _field_info->_static_field_size, "sanity");
6238   assert(ik->nonstatic_oop_map_count() == _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count,
6239          "sanity");
6240 
6241   assert(ik->is_instance_klass(), "sanity");
6242   assert(ik->size_helper() == _field_info->_instance_size, "sanity");
6243 
6244   // Fill in information already parsed
6245   ik->set_should_verify_class(_need_verify);
6246 
6247   // Not yet: supers are done below to support the new subtype-checking fields
6248   ik->set_nonstatic_field_size(_field_info->_nonstatic_field_size);
6249   ik->set_has_nonstatic_fields(_field_info->_has_nonstatic_fields);
6250   if (_field_info->_is_naturally_atomic && ik->is_value()) {
6251     ik->set_is_naturally_atomic();
6252   }
6253   if (_is_empty_inline_type) {
6254     ik->set_is_empty_inline_type();
6255   }
6256 
6257   if (this->_invalid_inline_super) {
6258     ik->set_invalid_inline_super();
6259   }
6260 
6261   if (_has_injected_identityObject) {
6262     ik->set_has_injected_identityObject();
6263   }
6264 
6265   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
6266   ik->set_static_oop_field_count(_fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + _fac->count[STATIC_INLINE]);
6267 
6268   // this transfers ownership of a lot of arrays from
6269   // the parser onto the InstanceKlass*
6270   apply_parsed_class_metadata(ik, _java_fields_count, CHECK);
6271 
6272   // can only set dynamic nest-host after static nest information is set
6273   if (cl_inst_info.dynamic_nest_host() != NULL) {
6274     ik->set_nest_host(cl_inst_info.dynamic_nest_host(), THREAD);
6275   }
6276 
6277   // note that is not safe to use the fields in the parser from this point on
6278   assert(NULL == _cp, "invariant");
6279   assert(NULL == _fields, "invariant");
6280   assert(NULL == _methods, "invariant");
6281   assert(NULL == _inner_classes, "invariant");
6282   assert(NULL == _nest_members, "invariant");
6283   assert(NULL == _combined_annotations, "invariant");
6284   assert(NULL == _record_components, "invariant");
6285   assert(NULL == _permitted_subclasses, "invariant");
6286 
6287   if (_has_final_method) {
6288     ik->set_has_final_method();
6289   }
6290 
6291   ik->copy_method_ordering(_method_ordering, CHECK);
6292   // The InstanceKlass::_methods_jmethod_ids cache
6293   // is managed on the assumption that the initial cache
6294   // size is equal to the number of methods in the class. If
6295   // that changes, then InstanceKlass::idnum_can_increment()
6296   // has to be changed accordingly.
6297   ik->set_initial_method_idnum(ik->methods()->length());
6298 
6299   ik->set_this_class_index(_this_class_index);
6300 
6301   if (_is_hidden || is_unsafe_anonymous()) {
6302     // _this_class_index is a CONSTANT_Class entry that refers to this
6303     // hidden or anonymous class itself. If this class needs to refer to its own
6304     // methods or fields, it would use a CONSTANT_MethodRef, etc, which would reference
6305     // _this_class_index. However, because this class is hidden or anonymous (it's
6306     // not stored in SystemDictionary), _this_class_index cannot be resolved
6307     // with ConstantPool::klass_at_impl, which does a SystemDictionary lookup.
6308     // Therefore, we must eagerly resolve _this_class_index now.
6309     ik->constants()->klass_at_put(_this_class_index, ik);
6310   }
6311 
6312   ik->set_minor_version(_minor_version);
6313   ik->set_major_version(_major_version);
6314   ik->set_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6315   ik->set_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6316   if (_is_declared_atomic) {
6317     ik->set_is_declared_atomic();
6318   }
6319 
6320   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6321     assert (ik->is_unsafe_anonymous(), "should be the same");
6322     ik->set_unsafe_anonymous_host(_unsafe_anonymous_host);
6323   }
6324   if (_is_hidden) {
6325     ik->set_is_hidden();
6326   }
6327 
6328   // Set PackageEntry for this_klass
6329   oop cl = ik->class_loader();
6330   Handle clh = Handle(THREAD, java_lang_ClassLoader::non_reflection_class_loader(cl));
6331   ClassLoaderData* cld = ClassLoaderData::class_loader_data_or_null(clh());
6332   ik->set_package(cld, NULL, CHECK);
6333 
6334   const Array<Method*>* const methods = ik->methods();
6335   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
6336   const int methods_len = methods->length();
6337 
6338   check_methods_for_intrinsics(ik, methods);
6339 
6340   // Fill in field values obtained by parse_classfile_attributes
6341   if (_parsed_annotations->has_any_annotations()) {
6342     _parsed_annotations->apply_to(ik);
6343   }
6344 
6345   apply_parsed_class_attributes(ik);
6346 
6347   // Miranda methods
6348   if ((_num_miranda_methods > 0) ||
6349       // if this class introduced new miranda methods or
6350       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_miranda_methods())
6351         // super class exists and this class inherited miranda methods
6352      ) {
6353        ik->set_has_miranda_methods(); // then set a flag
6354   }
6355 
6356   // Fill in information needed to compute superclasses.
6357   ik->initialize_supers(const_cast<InstanceKlass*>(_super_klass), _transitive_interfaces, CHECK);
6358   ik->set_transitive_interfaces(_transitive_interfaces);
6359   ik->set_local_interfaces(_local_interfaces);
6360   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6361   _local_interfaces = NULL;
6362 
6363   // Initialize itable offset tables
6364   klassItable::setup_itable_offset_table(ik);
6365 
6366   // Compute transitive closure of interfaces this class implements
6367   // Do final class setup
6368   OopMapBlocksBuilder* oop_map_blocks = _field_info->oop_map_blocks;
6369   if (oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
6370     oop_map_blocks->copy(ik->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps());
6371   }
6372 
6373   if (_has_contended_fields || _parsed_annotations->is_contended() ||
6374       ( _super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_contended_annotations())) {
6375     ik->set_has_contended_annotations(true);
6376   }
6377 
6378   // Fill in has_finalizer, has_vanilla_constructor, and layout_helper
6379   set_precomputed_flags(ik);
6380 
6381   // check if this class can access its super class
6382   check_super_class_access(ik, CHECK);
6383 
6384   // check if this class can access its superinterfaces
6385   check_super_interface_access(ik, CHECK);
6386 
6387   // check if this class overrides any final method
6388   check_final_method_override(ik, CHECK);
6389 
6390   // reject static interface methods prior to Java 8
6391   if (ik->is_interface() && _major_version < JAVA_8_VERSION) {
6392     check_illegal_static_method(ik, CHECK);
6393   }
6394 
6395   // Obtain this_klass' module entry
6396   ModuleEntry* module_entry = ik->module();
6397   assert(module_entry != NULL, "module_entry should always be set");
6398 
6399   // Obtain java.lang.Module
6400   Handle module_handle(THREAD, module_entry->module());
6401 
6402   // Allocate mirror and initialize static fields
6403   // The create_mirror() call will also call compute_modifiers()
6404   java_lang_Class::create_mirror(ik,
6405                                  Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
6406                                  module_handle,
6407                                  _protection_domain,
6408                                  cl_inst_info.class_data(),
6409                                  CHECK);
6410 
6411   assert(_all_mirandas != NULL, "invariant");
6412 
6413   // Generate any default methods - default methods are public interface methods
6414   // that have a default implementation.  This is new with Java 8.
6415   if (_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
6416     DefaultMethods::generate_default_methods(ik,
6417                                              _all_mirandas,
6418                                              CHECK);
6419   }
6420 
6421   // Add read edges to the unnamed modules of the bootstrap and app class loaders.
6422   if (changed_by_loadhook && !module_handle.is_null() && module_entry->is_named() &&
6423       !module_entry->has_default_read_edges()) {
6424     if (!module_entry->set_has_default_read_edges()) {
6425       // We won a potential race
6426       JvmtiExport::add_default_read_edges(module_handle, THREAD);
6427     }
6428   }
6429 
6430   int nfields = ik->java_fields_count();
6431   if (ik->is_value()) nfields++;
6432   for (int i = 0; i < nfields; i++) {
6433     if (ik->field_is_inline_type(i)) {
6434       Symbol* klass_name = ik->field_signature(i)->fundamental_name(CHECK);
6435       // Inline classes for instance fields must have been pre-loaded
6436       // Inline classes for static fields might not have been loaded yet
6437       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::find(klass_name,
6438           Handle(THREAD, ik->class_loader()),
6439           Handle(THREAD, ik->protection_domain()), CHECK);
6440       if (klass != NULL) {
6441         assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(), "Inline type expected");
6442         ik->set_value_field_klass(i, klass);
6443       }
6444       klass_name->decrement_refcount();
6445     } else
6446       if (is_inline_type() && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_FIELD_INTERNAL) != 0)
6447         && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_STATIC) != 0)) {
6448       ValueKlass::cast(ik)->set_default_value_offset(ik->field_offset(i));
6449     }
6450   }
6451 
6452   if (is_inline_type()) {
6453     ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(ik);
6454     if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
6455       vk->set_alignment(_alignment);
6456       vk->set_first_field_offset(_first_field_offset);
6457       vk->set_exact_size_in_bytes(_exact_size_in_bytes);
6458     } else {
6459       vk->set_first_field_offset(vk->first_field_offset_old());
6460     }
6461     ValueKlass::cast(ik)->initialize_calling_convention(CHECK);
6462   }
6463 
6464   ClassLoadingService::notify_class_loaded(ik, false /* not shared class */);
6465 
6466   if (!is_internal()) {
6467     if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, load)) {
6468       ResourceMark rm;
6469       const char* module_name = (module_entry->name() == NULL) ? UNNAMED_MODULE : module_entry->name()->as_C_string();
6470       ik->print_class_load_logging(_loader_data, module_name, _stream);
6471     }
6472 
6473     if (ik->minor_version() == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
6474         ik->major_version() == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
6475         log_is_enabled(Info, class, preview)) {
6476       ResourceMark rm;
6477       log_info(class, preview)("Loading class %s that depends on preview features (class file version %d.65535)",
6478                                ik->external_name(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
6479     }
6480 
6481     if (log_is_enabled(Debug, class, resolve))  {
6482       ResourceMark rm;
6483       // print out the superclass.
6484       const char * from = ik->external_name();
6485       if (ik->java_super() != NULL) {
6486         log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (super)",
6487                    from,
6488                    ik->java_super()->external_name());
6489       }
6490       // print out each of the interface classes referred to by this class.
6491       const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = ik->local_interfaces();
6492       if (local_interfaces != NULL) {
6493         const int length = local_interfaces->length();
6494         for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
6495           const InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
6496           const char * to = k->external_name();
6497           log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (interface)", from, to);
6498         }
6499       }
6500     }
6501   }
6502 
6503   JFR_ONLY(INIT_ID(ik);)
6504 
6505   // If we reach here, all is well.
6506   // Now remove the InstanceKlass* from the _klass_to_deallocate field
6507   // in order for it to not be destroyed in the ClassFileParser destructor.
6508   set_klass_to_deallocate(NULL);
6509 
6510   // it's official
6511   set_klass(ik);
6512 
6513   if (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6514     Universe::initialize_the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array(ik, CHECK);
6515   }
6516 
6517   debug_only(ik->verify();)
6518 }
6519 
6520 void ClassFileParser::update_class_name(Symbol* new_class_name) {
6521   // Decrement the refcount in the old name, since we're clobbering it.
6522   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6523 
6524   _class_name = new_class_name;
6525   // Increment the refcount of the new name.
6526   // Now the ClassFileParser owns this name and will decrement in
6527   // the destructor.
6528   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6529 }
6530 
6531 // For an unsafe anonymous class that is in the unnamed package, move it to its host class's
6532 // package by prepending its host class's package name to its class name and setting
6533 // its _class_name field.
6534 void ClassFileParser::prepend_host_package_name(const InstanceKlass* unsafe_anonymous_host, TRAPS) {
6535   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6536   assert(strrchr(_class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) == NULL,
6537          "Unsafe anonymous class should not be in a package");
6538   TempNewSymbol host_pkg_name =
6539     ClassLoader::package_from_class_name(unsafe_anonymous_host->name());
6540 
6541   if (host_pkg_name != NULL) {
6542     int host_pkg_len = host_pkg_name->utf8_length();
6543     int class_name_len = _class_name->utf8_length();
6544     int symbol_len = host_pkg_len + 1 + class_name_len;
6545     char* new_anon_name = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(char, symbol_len + 1);
6546     int n = os::snprintf(new_anon_name, symbol_len + 1, "%.*s/%.*s",
6547                          host_pkg_len, host_pkg_name->base(), class_name_len, _class_name->base());
6548     assert(n == symbol_len, "Unexpected number of characters in string");
6549 
6550     // Decrement old _class_name to avoid leaking.
6551     _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6552 
6553     // Create a symbol and update the anonymous class name.
6554     // The new class name is created with a refcount of one. When installed into the InstanceKlass,
6555     // it'll be two and when the ClassFileParser destructor runs, it'll go back to one and get deleted
6556     // when the class is unloaded.
6557     _class_name = SymbolTable::new_symbol(new_anon_name, symbol_len);
6558   }
6559 }
6560 
6561 // If the host class and the anonymous class are in the same package then do
6562 // nothing.  If the anonymous class is in the unnamed package then move it to its
6563 // host's package.  If the classes are in different packages then throw an IAE
6564 // exception.
6565 void ClassFileParser::fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(TRAPS) {
6566   assert(_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL, "Expected an unsafe anonymous class");
6567 
6568   const jbyte* anon_last_slash = UTF8::strrchr((const jbyte*)_class_name->base(),
6569                                                _class_name->utf8_length(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH);
6570   if (anon_last_slash == NULL) {  // Unnamed package
6571     prepend_host_package_name(_unsafe_anonymous_host, CHECK);
6572   } else {
6573     if (!_unsafe_anonymous_host->is_same_class_package(_unsafe_anonymous_host->class_loader(), _class_name)) {
6574       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6575       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalArgumentException(),
6576         err_msg("Host class %s and anonymous class %s are in different packages",
6577         _unsafe_anonymous_host->name()->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string()));
6578     }
6579   }
6580 }
6581 
6582 static bool relax_format_check_for(ClassLoaderData* loader_data) {
6583   bool trusted = loader_data->is_boot_class_loader_data() ||
6584                  loader_data->is_platform_class_loader_data();
6585   bool need_verify =
6586     // verifyAll
6587     (BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote) ||
6588     // verifyRemote
6589     (!BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote && !trusted);
6590   return !need_verify;
6591 }
6592 
6593 ClassFileParser::ClassFileParser(ClassFileStream* stream,
6594                                  Symbol* name,
6595                                  ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
6596                                  const ClassLoadInfo* cl_info,
6597                                  Publicity pub_level,
6598                                  TRAPS) :
6599   _stream(stream),
6600   _class_name(NULL),
6601   _loader_data(loader_data),
6602   _unsafe_anonymous_host(cl_info->unsafe_anonymous_host()),
6603   _cp_patches(cl_info->cp_patches()),
6604   _is_hidden(cl_info->is_hidden()),
6605   _can_access_vm_annotations(cl_info->can_access_vm_annotations()),
6606   _num_patched_klasses(0),
6607   _max_num_patched_klasses(0),
6608   _orig_cp_size(0),
6609   _first_patched_klass_resolved_index(0),
6610   _super_klass(),
6611   _cp(NULL),
6612   _fields(NULL),
6613   _methods(NULL),
6614   _inner_classes(NULL),
6615   _nest_members(NULL),
6616   _nest_host(0),
6617   _permitted_subclasses(NULL),
6618   _record_components(NULL),
6619   _temp_local_interfaces(NULL),
6620   _local_interfaces(NULL),
6621   _transitive_interfaces(NULL),
6622   _combined_annotations(NULL),
6623   _class_annotations(NULL),
6624   _class_type_annotations(NULL),
6625   _fields_annotations(NULL),
6626   _fields_type_annotations(NULL),
6627   _klass(NULL),
6628   _klass_to_deallocate(NULL),
6629   _parsed_annotations(NULL),
6630   _fac(NULL),
6631   _field_info(NULL),
6632   _method_ordering(NULL),
6633   _all_mirandas(NULL),
6634   _vtable_size(0),
6635   _itable_size(0),
6636   _num_miranda_methods(0),
6637   _rt(REF_NONE),
6638   _protection_domain(cl_info->protection_domain()),
6639   _access_flags(),
6640   _pub_level(pub_level),
6641   _bad_constant_seen(0),
6642   _synthetic_flag(false),
6643   _sde_length(false),
6644   _sde_buffer(NULL),
6645   _sourcefile_index(0),
6646   _generic_signature_index(0),
6647   _major_version(0),
6648   _minor_version(0),
6649   _this_class_index(0),
6650   _super_class_index(0),
6651   _itfs_len(0),
6652   _java_fields_count(0),
6653   _need_verify(false),
6654   _relax_verify(false),
6655   _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6656   _declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6657   _has_final_method(false),
6658   _has_contended_fields(false),
6659   _has_inline_type_fields(false),
6660   _has_nonstatic_fields(false),
6661   _is_empty_inline_type(false),
6662   _is_naturally_atomic(false),
6663   _is_declared_atomic(false),
6664   _invalid_inline_super(false),
6665   _invalid_identity_super(false),
6666   _implements_identityObject(false),
6667   _has_injected_identityObject(false),
6668   _has_finalizer(false),
6669   _has_empty_finalizer(false),
6670   _has_vanilla_constructor(false),
6671   _max_bootstrap_specifier_index(-1) {
6672 
6673   _class_name = name != NULL ? name : vmSymbols::unknown_class_name();
6674   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6675 
6676   assert(THREAD->is_Java_thread(), "invariant");
6677   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
6678   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6679   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
6680   assert(_stream->buffer() == _stream->current(), "invariant");
6681   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6682   assert(0 == _access_flags.as_int(), "invariant");
6683 
6684   // Figure out whether we can skip format checking (matching classic VM behavior)
6685   if (DumpSharedSpaces) {
6686     // verify == true means it's a 'remote' class (i.e., non-boot class)
6687     // Verification decision is based on BytecodeVerificationRemote flag
6688     // for those classes.
6689     _need_verify = (stream->need_verify()) ? BytecodeVerificationRemote :
6690                                               BytecodeVerificationLocal;
6691   }
6692   else {
6693     _need_verify = Verifier::should_verify_for(_loader_data->class_loader(),
6694                                                stream->need_verify());
6695   }
6696   if (_cp_patches != NULL) {
6697     int len = _cp_patches->length();
6698     for (int i=0; i<len; i++) {
6699       if (has_cp_patch_at(i)) {
6700         Handle patch = cp_patch_at(i);
6701         if (java_lang_String::is_instance(patch()) || java_lang_Class::is_instance(patch())) {
6702           // We need to append the names of the patched classes to the end of the constant pool,
6703           // because a patched class may have a Utf8 name that's not already included in the
6704           // original constant pool. These class names are used when patch_constant_pool()
6705           // calls patch_class().
6706           //
6707           // Note that a String in cp_patch_at(i) may be used to patch a Utf8, a String, or a Class.
6708           // At this point, we don't know the tag for index i yet, because we haven't parsed the
6709           // constant pool. So we can only assume the worst -- every String is used to patch a Class.
6710           _max_num_patched_klasses++;
6711         }
6712       }
6713     }
6714   }
6715 
6716   // synch back verification state to stream
6717   stream->set_verify(_need_verify);
6718 
6719   // Check if verification needs to be relaxed for this class file
6720   // Do not restrict it to jdk1.0 or jdk1.1 to maintain backward compatibility (4982376)
6721   _relax_verify = relax_format_check_for(_loader_data);
6722 
6723   parse_stream(stream, CHECK);
6724 
6725   post_process_parsed_stream(stream, _cp, CHECK);
6726 }
6727 
6728 void ClassFileParser::clear_class_metadata() {
6729   // metadata created before the instance klass is created.  Must be
6730   // deallocated if classfile parsing returns an error.
6731   _cp = NULL;
6732   _fields = NULL;
6733   _methods = NULL;
6734   _inner_classes = NULL;
6735   _nest_members = NULL;
6736   _permitted_subclasses = NULL;
6737   _combined_annotations = NULL;
6738   _class_annotations = _class_type_annotations = NULL;
6739   _fields_annotations = _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
6740   _record_components = NULL;
6741 }
6742 
6743 // Destructor to clean up
6744 ClassFileParser::~ClassFileParser() {
6745   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6746 
6747   if (_cp != NULL) {
6748     MetadataFactory::free_metadata(_loader_data, _cp);
6749   }
6750   if (_fields != NULL) {
6751     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _fields);
6752   }
6753 
6754   if (_methods != NULL) {
6755     // Free methods
6756     InstanceKlass::deallocate_methods(_loader_data, _methods);
6757   }
6758 
6759   // beware of the Universe::empty_blah_array!!
6760   if (_inner_classes != NULL && _inner_classes != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6761     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _inner_classes);
6762   }
6763 
6764   if (_nest_members != NULL && _nest_members != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6765     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _nest_members);
6766   }
6767 
6768   if (_record_components != NULL) {
6769     InstanceKlass::deallocate_record_components(_loader_data, _record_components);
6770   }
6771 
6772   if (_permitted_subclasses != NULL && _permitted_subclasses != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6773     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _permitted_subclasses);
6774   }
6775 
6776   // Free interfaces
6777   InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(_loader_data, _super_klass,
6778                                        _local_interfaces, _transitive_interfaces);
6779 
6780   if (_combined_annotations != NULL) {
6781     // After all annotations arrays have been created, they are installed into the
6782     // Annotations object that will be assigned to the InstanceKlass being created.
6783 
6784     // Deallocate the Annotations object and the installed annotations arrays.
6785     _combined_annotations->deallocate_contents(_loader_data);
6786 
6787     // If the _combined_annotations pointer is non-NULL,
6788     // then the other annotations fields should have been cleared.
6789     assert(_class_annotations       == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6790     assert(_class_type_annotations  == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6791     assert(_fields_annotations      == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6792     assert(_fields_type_annotations == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6793   } else {
6794     // If the annotations arrays were not installed into the Annotations object,
6795     // then they have to be deallocated explicitly.
6796     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_annotations);
6797     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_type_annotations);
6798     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_annotations);
6799     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_type_annotations);
6800   }
6801 
6802   clear_class_metadata();
6803   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6804   _local_interfaces = NULL;
6805 
6806   // deallocate the klass if already created.  Don't directly deallocate, but add
6807   // to the deallocate list so that the klass is removed from the CLD::_klasses list
6808   // at a safepoint.
6809   if (_klass_to_deallocate != NULL) {
6810     _loader_data->add_to_deallocate_list(_klass_to_deallocate);
6811   }
6812 }
6813 
6814 void ClassFileParser::parse_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
6815                                    TRAPS) {
6816 
6817   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6818   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6819 
6820   // BEGIN STREAM PARSING
6821   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // magic, major, minor
6822   // Magic value
6823   const u4 magic = stream->get_u4_fast();
6824   guarantee_property(magic == JAVA_CLASSFILE_MAGIC,
6825                      "Incompatible magic value %u in class file %s",
6826                      magic, CHECK);
6827 
6828   // Version numbers
6829   _minor_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6830   _major_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6831 
6832   if (DumpSharedSpaces && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6833     ResourceMark rm;
6834     warning("Pre JDK 6 class not supported by CDS: %u.%u %s",
6835             _major_version,  _minor_version, _class_name->as_C_string());
6836     Exceptions::fthrow(
6837       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6838       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
6839       "Unsupported major.minor version for dump time %u.%u",
6840       _major_version,
6841       _minor_version);
6842   }
6843 
6844   // Check version numbers - we check this even with verifier off
6845   verify_class_version(_major_version, _minor_version, _class_name, CHECK);
6846 
6847   stream->guarantee_more(3, CHECK); // length, first cp tag
6848   u2 cp_size = stream->get_u2_fast();
6849 
6850   guarantee_property(
6851     cp_size >= 1, "Illegal constant pool size %u in class file %s",
6852     cp_size, CHECK);
6853 
6854   _orig_cp_size = cp_size;
6855   if (is_hidden()) { // Add a slot for hidden class name.
6856     assert(_max_num_patched_klasses == 0, "Sanity check");
6857     cp_size++;
6858   } else {
6859     if (int(cp_size) + _max_num_patched_klasses > 0xffff) {
6860       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_InternalError(), "not enough space for patched classes");
6861     }
6862     cp_size += _max_num_patched_klasses;
6863   }
6864 
6865   _cp = ConstantPool::allocate(_loader_data,
6866                                cp_size,
6867                                CHECK);
6868 
6869   ConstantPool* const cp = _cp;
6870 
6871   parse_constant_pool(stream, cp, _orig_cp_size, CHECK);
6872 
6873   assert(cp_size == (const u2)cp->length(), "invariant");
6874 
6875   // ACCESS FLAGS
6876   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // flags, this_class, super_class, infs_len
6877 
6878   jint recognized_modifiers = JVM_RECOGNIZED_CLASS_MODIFIERS;
6879   // JVM_ACC_MODULE is defined in JDK-9 and later.
6880   if (_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION) {
6881     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_MODULE;
6882   }
6883   // JVM_ACC_VALUE is defined for class file version 55 and later
6884   if (supports_inline_types()) {
6885     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_VALUE;
6886   }
6887 
6888   // Access flags
6889   jint flags = stream->get_u2_fast() & recognized_modifiers;
6890 
6891   if ((flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE) && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6892     // Set abstract bit for old class files for backward compatibility
6893     flags |= JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT;
6894   }
6895 
6896   verify_legal_class_modifiers(flags, CHECK);
6897 
6898   short bad_constant = class_bad_constant_seen();
6899   if (bad_constant != 0) {
6900     // Do not throw CFE until after the access_flags are checked because if
6901     // ACC_MODULE is set in the access flags, then NCDFE must be thrown, not CFE.
6902     classfile_parse_error("Unknown constant tag %u in class file %s", bad_constant, CHECK);
6903   }
6904 
6905   _access_flags.set_flags(flags);
6906 
6907   // This class and superclass
6908   _this_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6909   check_property(
6910     valid_cp_range(_this_class_index, cp_size) &&
6911       cp->tag_at(_this_class_index).is_unresolved_klass(),
6912     "Invalid this class index %u in constant pool in class file %s",
6913     _this_class_index, CHECK);
6914 
6915   Symbol* const class_name_in_cp = cp->klass_name_at(_this_class_index);
6916   assert(class_name_in_cp != NULL, "class_name can't be null");
6917 
6918   // Don't need to check whether this class name is legal or not.
6919   // It has been checked when constant pool is parsed.
6920   // However, make sure it is not an array type.
6921   if (_need_verify) {
6922     guarantee_property(class_name_in_cp->char_at(0) != JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY,
6923                        "Bad class name in class file %s",
6924                        CHECK);
6925   }
6926 
6927 #ifdef ASSERT
6928   // Basic sanity checks
6929   assert(!(_is_hidden && (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL)), "mutually exclusive variants");
6930 
6931   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6932     assert(_class_name == vmSymbols::unknown_class_name(), "A named anonymous class???");
6933   }
6934   if (_is_hidden) {
6935     assert(_class_name != vmSymbols::unknown_class_name(), "hidden classes should have a special name");
6936   }
6937 #endif
6938 
6939   // Update the _class_name as needed depending on whether this is a named,
6940   // un-named, hidden or unsafe-anonymous class.
6941 
6942   if (_is_hidden) {
6943     assert(_class_name != NULL, "Unexpected null _class_name");
6944 #ifdef ASSERT
6945     if (_need_verify) {
6946       verify_legal_class_name(_class_name, CHECK);
6947     }
6948 #endif
6949 
6950   // NOTE: !_is_hidden does not imply "findable" as it could be an old-style
6951   //       "hidden" unsafe-anonymous class
6952 
6953   // If this is an anonymous class fix up its name if it is in the unnamed
6954   // package.  Otherwise, throw IAE if it is in a different package than
6955   // its host class.
6956   } else if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6957     update_class_name(class_name_in_cp);
6958     fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(CHECK);
6959 
6960   } else {
6961     // Check if name in class file matches given name
6962     if (_class_name != class_name_in_cp) {
6963       if (_class_name != vmSymbols::unknown_class_name()) {
6964         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6965         Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6966                            vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
6967                            "%s (wrong name: %s)",
6968                            class_name_in_cp->as_C_string(),
