6969                            _class_name->as_C_string()
6970                            );
6971         return;
6972       } else {
6973         // The class name was not known by the caller so we set it from
6974         // the value in the CP.
6975         update_class_name(class_name_in_cp);
6976       }
6977       // else nothing to do: the expected class name matches what is in the CP
6978     }
6979   }
6980 
6981   // Verification prevents us from creating names with dots in them, this
6982   // asserts that that's the case.
6983   assert(is_internal_format(_class_name), "external class name format used internally");
6984 
6985   if (!is_internal()) {
6986     LogTarget(Debug, class, preorder) lt;
6987     if (lt.is_enabled()){
6988       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6989       LogStream ls(lt);
6990       ls.print("%s", _class_name->as_klass_external_name());
6991       if (stream->source() != NULL) {
6992         ls.print(" source: %s", stream->source());
6993       }
6994       ls.cr();
6995     }
6996 
6997 #if INCLUDE_CDS
6998     if (DumpLoadedClassList != NULL && stream->source() != NULL && classlist_file->is_open()) {
6999       if (!ClassLoader::has_jrt_entry()) {
7000         warning("DumpLoadedClassList and CDS are not supported in exploded build");
7001         DumpLoadedClassList = NULL;
7002       } else if (SystemDictionaryShared::is_sharing_possible(_loader_data) &&
7003                  !_is_hidden &&
7004                  _unsafe_anonymous_host == NULL) {
7005         // Only dump the classes that can be stored into CDS archive.
7006         // Hidden and unsafe anonymous classes such as generated LambdaForm classes are also not included.
7007         oop class_loader = _loader_data->class_loader();
7008         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7009         bool skip = false;
7010         if (class_loader == NULL || SystemDictionary::is_platform_class_loader(class_loader)) {
7011           // For the boot and platform class loaders, skip classes that are not found in the
7012           // java runtime image, such as those found in the --patch-module entries.
7013           // These classes can't be loaded from the archive during runtime.
7014           if (!stream->from_boot_loader_modules_image() && strncmp(stream->source(), "jrt:", 4) != 0) {
7015             skip = true;
7016           }
7017 
7018           if (class_loader == NULL && ClassLoader::contains_append_entry(stream->source())) {
7019             // .. but don't skip the boot classes that are loaded from -Xbootclasspath/a
7020             // as they can be loaded from the archive during runtime.
7021             skip = false;
7022           }
7023         }
7024         if (skip) {
7025           tty->print_cr("skip writing class %s from source %s to classlist file",
7026             _class_name->as_C_string(), stream->source());
7027         } else {
7028           classlist_file->print_cr("%s", _class_name->as_C_string());
7029           classlist_file->flush();
7030         }
7031       }
7032     }
7033 #endif
7034   }
7035 
7036   // SUPERKLASS
7037   _super_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
7038   _super_klass = parse_super_class(cp,
7039                                    _super_class_index,
7040                                    _need_verify,
7041                                    CHECK);
7042 
7043   // Interfaces
7044   _itfs_len = stream->get_u2_fast();
7045   parse_interfaces(stream,
7046                    _itfs_len,
7047                    cp,
7048                    is_inline_type(),
7049                    &_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
7050                    &_is_declared_atomic,
7051                    CHECK);
7052 
7053   assert(_temp_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7054 
7055   // Fields (offsets are filled in later)
7056   _fac = new FieldAllocationCount();
7057   parse_fields(stream,
7058                is_interface(),
7059                is_inline_type(),
7060                _fac,
7061                cp,
7062                cp_size,
7063                &_java_fields_count,
7064                CHECK);
7065 
7066   assert(_fields != NULL, "invariant");
7067 
7068   // Methods
7069   AccessFlags promoted_flags;
7070   parse_methods(stream,
7071                 is_interface(),
7072                 is_inline_type(),
7073                 &promoted_flags,
7074                 &_has_final_method,
7075                 &_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
7076                 CHECK);
7077 
7078   assert(_methods != NULL, "invariant");
7079 
7080   // promote flags from parse_methods() to the klass' flags
7081   _access_flags.add_promoted_flags(promoted_flags.as_int());
7082 
7083   if (_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
7084     _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
7085   }
7086 
7087   // Additional attributes/annotations
7088   _parsed_annotations = new ClassAnnotationCollector();
7089   parse_classfile_attributes(stream, cp, _parsed_annotations, CHECK);
7090 
7091   assert(_inner_classes != NULL, "invariant");
7092 
7093   // Finalize the Annotations metadata object,
7094   // now that all annotation arrays have been created.
7095   create_combined_annotations(CHECK);
7096 
7097   // Make sure this is the end of class file stream
7098   guarantee_property(stream->at_eos(),
7099                      "Extra bytes at the end of class file %s",
7100                      CHECK);
7101 
7102   // all bytes in stream read and parsed
7103 }
7104 
7105 void ClassFileParser::mangle_hidden_class_name(InstanceKlass* const ik) {
7106   ResourceMark rm;
7107   // Construct hidden name from _class_name, "+", and &ik. Note that we can't
7108   // use a '/' because that confuses finding the class's package.  Also, can't
7109   // use an illegal char such as ';' because that causes serialization issues
7110   // and issues with hidden classes that create their own hidden classes.
7111   char addr_buf[20];
7112   jio_snprintf(addr_buf, 20, INTPTR_FORMAT, p2i(ik));
7113   size_t new_name_len = _class_name->utf8_length() + 2 + strlen(addr_buf);
7114   char* new_name = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(char, new_name_len);
7115   jio_snprintf(new_name, new_name_len, "%s+%s",
7116                _class_name->as_C_string(), addr_buf);
7117   update_class_name(SymbolTable::new_symbol(new_name));
7118 
7119   // Add a Utf8 entry containing the hidden name.
7120   assert(_class_name != NULL, "Unexpected null _class_name");
7121   int hidden_index = _orig_cp_size; // this is an extra slot we added
7122   _cp->symbol_at_put(hidden_index, _class_name);
7123 
7124   // Update this_class_index's slot in the constant pool with the new Utf8 entry.
7125   // We have to update the resolved_klass_index and the name_index together
7126   // so extract the existing resolved_klass_index first.
7127   CPKlassSlot cp_klass_slot = _cp->klass_slot_at(_this_class_index);
7128   int resolved_klass_index = cp_klass_slot.resolved_klass_index();
7129   _cp->unresolved_klass_at_put(_this_class_index, hidden_index, resolved_klass_index);
7130   assert(_cp->klass_slot_at(_this_class_index).name_index() == _orig_cp_size,
7131          "Bad name_index");
7132 }
7133 
7134 void ClassFileParser::post_process_parsed_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
7135                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
7136                                                  TRAPS) {
7137   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
7138   assert(stream->at_eos(), "invariant");
7139   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
7140   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
7141 
7142   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
7143     check_property(_temp_local_interfaces->length() == 0,
7144         "java.lang.Object cannot implement an interface in class file %s",
7145         CHECK);
7146   }
7147   // We check super class after class file is parsed and format is checked
7148   if (_super_class_index > 0 && NULL ==_super_klass) {
7149     Symbol* const super_class_name = cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index);
7150     if (is_interface()) {
7151       // Before attempting to resolve the superclass, check for class format
7152       // errors not checked yet.
7153       guarantee_property(super_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object(),
7154         "Interfaces must have java.lang.Object as superclass in class file %s",
7155         CHECK);
7156     }
7157     Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
7158     _super_klass = (const InstanceKlass*)
7159                        SystemDictionary::resolve_super_or_fail(_class_name,
7160                                                                super_class_name,
7161                                                                loader,
7162                                                                _protection_domain,
7163                                                                true,
7164                                                                CHECK);
7165   }
7166 
7167   if (_super_klass != NULL) {
7168     if (_super_klass->has_nonstatic_concrete_methods()) {
7169       _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
7170     }
7171     if (_super_klass->is_declared_atomic()) {
7172       _is_declared_atomic = true;
7173     }
7174 
7175     if (_super_klass->is_interface()) {
7176       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7177       Exceptions::fthrow(
7178         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
7179         vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
7180         "class %s has interface %s as super class",
7181         _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7182         _super_klass->external_name()
7183       );
7184       return;
7185     }
7186 
7187     // For an inline class, only java/lang/Object or special abstract classes
7188     // are acceptable super classes.
7189     if (is_inline_type()) {
7190       const InstanceKlass* super_ik = _super_klass;
7191       if (super_ik->invalid_inline_super()) {
7192         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7193         Exceptions::fthrow(
7194           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
7195           vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
7196           "inline class %s has an invalid super class %s",
7197           _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7198           _super_klass->external_name());
7199         return;
7200       }
7201     }
7202   }
7203 
7204   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_NonTearable() && _loader_data->class_loader() == NULL) {
7205     // This is the original source of this condition.
7206     // It propagates by inheritance, as if testing "instanceof NonTearable".
7207     _is_declared_atomic = true;
7208   } else if (*ForceNonTearable != '\0') {
7209     // Allow a command line switch to force the same atomicity property:
7210     const char* class_name_str = _class_name->as_C_string();
7211     if (StringUtils::class_list_match(ForceNonTearable, class_name_str)) {
7212       _is_declared_atomic = true;
7213     }
7214   }
7215 
7216   // Set ik->invalid_inline_super field to TRUE if already marked as invalid,
7217   // if super is marked invalid, or if is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()
7218   // returns true
7219   if (invalid_inline_super() ||
7220       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->invalid_inline_super()) ||
7221       is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()) {
7222     set_invalid_inline_super();
7223   }
7224 
7225   if (!is_inline_type() && invalid_inline_super() && (_super_klass == NULL || !_super_klass->invalid_inline_super())
7226       && !_implements_identityObject && class_name() != vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
7227     _temp_local_interfaces->append(SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass());
7228     _has_injected_identityObject = true;
7229   }
7230   int itfs_len = _temp_local_interfaces->length();
7231   if (itfs_len == 0) {
7232     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
7233   } else if (itfs_len == 1 && _temp_local_interfaces->at(0) == SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass()) {
7234     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array();
7235   } else {
7236     _local_interfaces = MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(_loader_data, itfs_len, NULL, CHECK);
7237     for (int i = 0; i < itfs_len; i++) {
7238       _local_interfaces->at_put(i, _temp_local_interfaces->at(i));
7239     }
7240   }
7241   _temp_local_interfaces = NULL;
7242   assert(_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7243 
7244   // Compute the transitive list of all unique interfaces implemented by this class
7245   _transitive_interfaces =
7246     compute_transitive_interfaces(_super_klass,
7247                                   _local_interfaces,
7248                                   _loader_data,
7249                                   CHECK);
7250 
7251   assert(_transitive_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7252 
7253   // sort methods
7254   _method_ordering = sort_methods(_methods);
7255 
7256   _all_mirandas = new GrowableArray<Method*>(20);
7257 
7258   Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
7259   klassVtable::compute_vtable_size_and_num_mirandas(&_vtable_size,
7260                                                     &_num_miranda_methods,
7261                                                     _all_mirandas,
7262                                                     _super_klass,
7263                                                     _methods,
7264                                                     _access_flags,
7265                                                     _major_version,
7266                                                     loader,
7267                                                     _class_name,
7268                                                     _local_interfaces,
7269                                                     CHECK);
7270 
7271   // Size of Java itable (in words)
7272   _itable_size = is_interface() ? 0 :
7273     klassItable::compute_itable_size(_transitive_interfaces);
7274 
7275   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
7276   assert(_parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
7277 
7278 
7279   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
7280     if (Signature::basic_type(fs.signature()) == T_VALUETYPE  && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
7281       // Pre-load inline class
7282       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::resolve_inline_type_field_or_fail(&fs,
7283           Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
7284           _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
7285       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
7286       assert(klass->access_flags().is_inline_type(), "Value type expected");
7287     }
7288   }
7289 
7290   _field_info = new FieldLayoutInfo();
7291   if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
7292     FieldLayoutBuilder lb(class_name(), super_klass(), _cp, _fields,
7293         _parsed_annotations->is_contended(), is_inline_type(),
7294         loader_data(), _protection_domain, _field_info);
7295     lb.build_layout(CHECK);
7296     if (is_inline_type()) {
7297       _alignment = lb.get_alignment();
7298       _first_field_offset = lb.get_first_field_offset();
7299       _exact_size_in_bytes = lb.get_exact_size_in_byte();
7300     }
7301   } else {
7302     layout_fields(cp, _fac, _parsed_annotations, _field_info, CHECK);
7303   }
7304   _has_inline_type_fields = _field_info->_has_inline_fields;
7305 
7306   // Compute reference type
7307   _rt = (NULL ==_super_klass) ? REF_NONE : _super_klass->reference_type();
7308 }
7309 
7310 void ClassFileParser::set_klass(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7311 
7312 #ifdef ASSERT
7313   if (klass != NULL) {
7314     assert(NULL == _klass, "leaking?");
7315   }
7316 #endif
7317 
7318   _klass = klass;
7319 }
7320 
7321 void ClassFileParser::set_klass_to_deallocate(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7322 
7323 #ifdef ASSERT
7324   if (klass != NULL) {
7325     assert(NULL == _klass_to_deallocate, "leaking?");
7326   }
7327 #endif
7328 
7329   _klass_to_deallocate = klass;
7330 }
7331 
7332 // Caller responsible for ResourceMark
7333 // clone stream with rewound position
7334 const ClassFileStream* ClassFileParser::clone_stream() const {
7335   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
7336 
7337   return _stream->clone();
7338 }

7340 // ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
7341 // debugging
7342 
7343 #ifdef ASSERT
7344 
7345 // return true if class_name contains no '.' (internal format is '/')
7346 bool ClassFileParser::is_internal_format(Symbol* class_name) {
7347   if (class_name != NULL) {
7348     ResourceMark rm;
7349     char* name = class_name->as_C_string();
7350     return strchr(name, JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT) == NULL;
7351   } else {
7352     return true;
7353   }
7354 }

7356 #endif
